Current Affairs Commentary

The Situation Can Still Be Managed

Rehe, with its vast area of 580,000 square miles, was lost to enemy forces of only two divisions in ten days. It goes without saying that it was a retreat without a fight, a desertion by someone. Only recently has there been news of Sun Dianying's troops engaging the enemy in fierce fighting in the Weichang area, with attempts to counterattack Chengde and restore Rehe. We are sincerely pleased to hear of the bravery of Sun's troops from afar, but we also expected that a part of the army would be isolated outside the border, with Chifeng and Chengde both belonging to the enemy. How could it last for a long time? In the past, driving hungry troops to battle, there were indeed those who were motivated by loyalty and righteousness for a time, but in the end, they did not help the overall situation of the country. Now, Sun's troops have also been reported to have retreated to Duolun.

Therefore, if our country is willing to retreat in defeat, then so be it. But if it still wants to recover lost territory, it should launch a sudden attack, taking advantage of the fact that the forced troops are still struggling to fight hard and the enemy has not yet established a firm foothold. Rapidly dispatch troops to provide assistance and launch a pincer attack with the troops outside the pass. At this time, the enemy troops defending Chengde consist of only one infantry brigade and one cavalry brigade from the Eighth Division, and those who can provide support are at most the entire Sixth Division and the Fourth Cavalry Brigade. Even if the original old troops of the Northeast Army are used, it would be enough to shatter the enemy. Therefore, today's bold advance without hesitation is the best strategy. Otherwise, detour through Zhangbei, fully supply the troops currently confronting the enemy. On the one hand, strictly control Gubeikou, on the other hand, order the anti-Japanese troops to concentrate in Duolun, and attack at any time, gradually recovering the area. Use our strengths to maximize the effectiveness of infantry sniping. The enemy has no convenient transportation and is in danger of being attacked. If we can hold on for a long time, even if we cannot recover Rehe, we can at least maintain Tianjin and Beiping, stabilize North China, which would still be a good strategy. If we are confused by the enemy's propaganda of bombing threats and the cunning plan to establish a neutral zone along the Great Wall, and do not adopt these two strategies, once Duolun falls into the hands of the enemy, the anti-Japanese troops will repeat the mistakes of Suma, and the situation in Chahar will be dangerous, and North China will fall into even greater danger. This is the worst of all strategies.

In order to complete its militaristic aggression, Japan does not hesitate to openly declare that Japan will expand its military, exposing the mask of the Geneva Disarmament Conference. Japan's increase in military equipment can be known from its fiscal military expenditure this year. The reason why it notified the League of Nations is that although Rehe has been obtained, it is not easy to defend. Disrupting Tianjin and Beiping still requires planning. If we examine the situation in Rehe and look at the map, we can see that the Greater Khingan Mountains pass through its northeast, and the Qilaotu Mountains originate from the Greater Khingan Mountains and meander south. The central part of Rehe is the highest point, crossing the Great Wall to form the Luan River valley, which flows directly into the Bohai Sea. Sloping to the east is the [South Manchurian] Plain, and sloping to the west is the Hebei-Shandong alluvial land. According to this topography, if we can control Rehe and advance eastward, it would be very easy to follow the terrain to recover the Northeast. Unfortunately, if Rehe is taken by the enemy, they can control Luandong along the Luan River, looking down from a high position, Hebei will be in danger. Therefore, since the fall of Rehe, the offense and defense have been reversed, and the enemy is already in an advantageous position. Fortunately, Chahar is still in our hands, and [Duolun] can still control the enemy's flank. If our country can make timely efforts to set up defenses along the border and gather heavy troops in Duolun, resolving the past issues between Inner and Outer Mongolia in the shortest possible time, then attacking Rehe from the side and recovering lost territory is not necessarily impossible. In short, losing the Northeast was a mistake in the past, and abandoning Rehe was another mistake later. The court and the public should reflect on this and avoid repeating past mistakes. There is no need to blame those who cannot be blamed. We must immediately rise up to resist Japan, and any sacrifice will be made to stop the enemy's continuous attacks and save the country from danger. The Tianjin and Beiping telegrams received today seem to have decided to resist unanimously. The only hope for the renewal of China lies in this.

Enemy Troops Plan to Defend Luanping Firmly

(Beiping) Gubeikou report: Large numbers of our volunteer troops are attacking the enemy in the Lingyuan to Pingquan area, and the fighting is fierce. Both sides have suffered heavy casualties. It is said that the enemy is very concerned about the rear and will defend Luanping firmly in order to clear the volunteer troops in the rear. However, we have decided to launch a strike with the volunteer troops. (10th Dispatch)

Qingshiliang Shoots Down Japanese Aircraft

(Beiping) Yesterday afternoon, at 5 PM, three enemy planes flew from Chengde to bomb our rear positions at Gubeikou. Our Gubeikou garrison fired at them with anti-aircraft machine guns. One plane was hit and fled. The remaining two planes fled to the Qingshiliang area to bomb our army's positions. Our army shot down one plane with anti-aircraft artillery. The fuselage crashed into the mountain, and the damage was very heavy. The enemy pilot Hirota was crushed in the head by the plane and died immediately. There were also three other crew members, including Sergeant Sasaki, who were all captured and escorted to the rear. The plane was transported to Gubeikou. More than a hundred anti-aircraft artillery pieces and anti-aircraft machine guns were transported to our front and rear positions, greatly boosting morale. (10th Dispatch)

Sun Dianying's Troops Retreat to Duolun Due to Lack of Supplies

Telegram from Tianjin Recounts the Counterattack Process

(Tianjin) Front-line telegram: Sun Dianying's troops began to retreat from Weichang to Duolun on the 9th due to the exhaustion of ammunition and supplies and the inability to replenish them. (10th Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Sun Dianying telegraphed from Tianjin on the 8th during the retreat, saying: "At midnight on the 8th, east of Weichang, Liu Brigade bravely attacked the enemy's rear, followed by a full-scale counterattack by the main force. Deputy Army Commanders Jin and Yu and Brigade Commander Liu supervised the battle. The fighting was extremely fierce. Our Battalion Commander Wu Xiangsheng was captured, and Battalion Commander Zhang Chengwuzhen died in battle. Battalion Commanders Liu Shenxiu and Diao Songting were injured. Six company commanders died in battle, and more than thirty platoon commanders were injured. Soldiers killed in battle exceeded two hundred. Injured company and platoon commanders will be reported after verification. More than thirty enemies were captured, and more than four hundred were killed. Two Type 6 mountain guns and two machine guns were captured. The number of rifles and horses captured and lost will be reported after verification. Now, I am retreating slightly to the rear. Our army is currently reorganizing and pursuing." (10th Dispatch)

(Beiping) The troops defending Gubeikou and Sun's troops in the regiment training ground are fighting extremely fiercely, but they are in dire need of supplies and medicine. Automobile fuel is also in great demand. Efforts are currently being made to provide relief. (10th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Sun Dianying sent a telegram to Beiping this morning, reporting that the Ding Brigade under his command was in fierce fighting with the enemy in Haolitudou, and he personally led troops to provide assistance. After more than ten hours of fierce fighting, the enemy began to rout. The enemy suffered heavy casualties, and two tanks and more than twenty machine guns were captured, as well as a large amount of ammunition and supplies. Our Battalion Commander Wu of the Ding Brigade died in battle. The number of officers and soldiers killed, wounded, and frozen to death has reached more than a thousand. Outside Xifengkou, our army is still guarding Baishelazishan and Dayaocheng, and there has been no fierce fighting for days. (10th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Fan Changling, the Magistrate of Weichang County, telegraphed to Beiping on the 9th, saying that according to reports, a large number of Japanese plainclothes teams had infiltrated the city of Weichang County, attempting to undermine our military's morale. Zheng Xiaoxu to Be Scorned by the Japanese

Lord Lytton on Japan's Withdrawal from the League of Nations

The League of Nations Cannot Delay Its Actions Because of This

Diplomatic Contacts Should Be Made to Exert Pressure on Japan

(London) Lord Lytton published an article in the "Observer," stating that Japan's withdrawal from the League of Nations must not be a reason for the League of Nations to delay its actions. If Japan does withdraw from the League of Nations, diplomatic contacts should be made immediately to uphold the League of Nations Covenant, and such contacts must be supplemented by gradually effective means of pressure, such as prohibiting loans to Japan and providing loans. Ultimately, Manchuria should be given an effective government that does not conflict with the Covenant and is acceptable to the people. However, this matter cannot be realized without Japan's support. Therefore, the pressure on Japan to force it to recognize the League of Nations' arbitration must proceed simultaneously with another solution prepared by the League of Nations. (10th Reuters Dispatch)

Ambassador Yan Huiqing Presents Credentials to Russia

Promoting Friendly Sino-Russian Relations

(Moscow) Dr. Yan Huiqing, Chinese Ambassador to the Soviet Union, presented his credentials to Kalinin, Chairman of the Central Executive Committee of the Soviet Union, today. The ceremony took place in the Kremlin. Those participating included Litvinov, Karakhan, and Koenlovsky. After finishing his speech, Yan introduced the embassy staff to Kalinin. Afterwards, the two had a private conversation. Yan's speech stated: "I am deeply gratified by the restoration of the old friendship between China and the Soviet Union, and I am especially pleased to be able to work for the relations between the two countries. China and the Soviet Union are not only geographically connected, but also have historical and political relations. We have thousands of miles of border. Your country, based on the principles of equality and mutual assistance, signed the important Beijing Agreement of 1924 with the Chinese government. Your country, during the transition and transformation period, has been able to establish a

Ambassador Yan Huiqing

an economic plan with great frugality and dedication, put it into practice, and gained multi-faceted admiration. The success of this plan and its implementation will surely be an inspiration to the Chinese government and people who are also engaged in transformation work. Therefore, I will do my best to promote the traditional friendship and friendly relations between our two countries." Kalinin replied, "The Soviet government has always adhered to the basic spirit of the important declarations of 1919 and 1920 and the Beijing Agreement of 1924 in its relations with China. The Soviet Union's policy has never changed. Even in recent years, when diplomatic relations have been suspended due to other reasons, its friendship and sympathy for China have not changed." Finally, Kalinin expressed his deep satisfaction with the resumption of Sino-Soviet relations, and said that Ambassador Yan would surely gain the trust and support of the Soviet government in fulfilling his mission. (9th Tass Dispatch)

Guo Taiqi's Remarks

Japan's Ambitions Toward Us Have Not Ended

Further Strengthen China's Determination to Resist Japan

(London) Guo Taiqi, Chinese representative to the League of Nations and Minister to the United Kingdom, returned here from Geneva yesterday. This afternoon, a reporter from this agency visited him. Minister Guo said: "There is no such thing as direct negotiations between China and Japan, because it is contrary to the policy China holds, and Japan has now occupied Rehe and its ambitions have not ended. Its intention is to conquer all of China and dominate Asia. Therefore, direct negotiations at this time are also useless. Chinese public opinion is extremely angry. Although Rehe has been lost, it will surely be recovered. This is predictable. Although there is no official news to confirm the death of Tang Yulin and the resignation of Zhang Xueliang, from now on, the anti-Japanese military affairs will be personally directed by Chiang Kai-shek, and the people of the whole country will be united to support him. Although Guangzhou and Nanjing had slightly different opinions on politics in the past, they have now abandoned their past grievances and are united against foreign enemies. The only thing they disagree on is the method to be adopted in national defense. Therefore, China is being unified by the pressure of foreign aggression. I am personally deeply disappointed by the defeat of the Chinese army, but although the war is temporarily unfavorable, the morale of the people is still available. From now on, the people's sense of self-defense will be even greater than before. Therefore, the loss of Rehe has further strengthened China's determination to resist to the end. The League of Nations' report is very clear about Japan's actions. However, the Japanese government took advantage of the report to invade Rehe Province after it was passed by the General Assembly, and staged further acts of aggression. In this situation, it is even more necessary than before for the international community to exert diplomatic and economic pressure on Japan. And our people have the right to boycott enemy goods so that they will not be dumped on our markets." As Minister Guo was about to finish his speech, he mentioned that the issue of banning arms exports would be discussed in Geneva, saying, "I sincerely hope for the success of the Disarmament Conference, but I personally believe that this conference has little hope. If Japan does not withdraw from Chinese territory for one day, China will not be able to sign the disarmament treaty for one day. The Tokyo government will also refuse to sign. In this situation, how can the naval reductions demanded by the great powers be achieved? I am afraid that the Disarmament Conference will be shelved from now on." A certain British radio company will invite Guo Taiqi and Yosuke Matsuoka to speak on the Sino-Japanese dispute on Saturday. (9th Havas Dispatch)

Inspector General of Customs Advocates Revising the Yangtze River Trade Regulations

(Nanjing) Previously, the Ministry of Finance received a request from Jia Yanlin, Superintendent of the Zhenhai Customs, to add branch customs in Lujing Port and Jiangyin. After investigation by the Inspector General of Customs, the Yangtze River Trade Regulations were formulated by the Qing Dynasty. Now, the regular customs and tax bureaus have been abolished, and there are no inspection agencies below Zhenjiang. If cargo ships are allowed to unload at will downstream of Zhenjiang, it will be impossible to prevent. The Yangtze River Trade Regulations should be revised to prevent ships from freely entering the river for trade. Patrol boats should be used to patrol the river mouth. Any merchant ship entering the Yangtze River should first apply to the Wusong Customs for a permit. Those sailing from the Yangtze River for export should also apply for approval from the Wusong Customs. It is also planned to build three Type B patrol boats, using Wusong as a base, and distribute them in the Yangtze River for patrol, from the coast to Jiangyin and the north and south mouths of the Yangtze River on Chongming Island. Once the trade regulations are revised and the coastal patrol boats are built, it will be enough to prevent ships from directly entering the Yangtze River and privately loading and unloading goods in the interior. Therefore, there is no need to set up separate customs offices in Jiangyin and Lujing Port. The Ministry of Finance yesterday instructed the Zhenhai Customs to inform them that there is no need to set up separate customs offices. (10th Dispatch)

Constitutional Draft Review Committee

Decides on the Rights and Obligations of the People

(Nanjing) The second group of the Constitutional Draft Committee held its third review meeting at 3:00 PM on the 10th. Wu Jingxiong presided over the meeting. Committee members Ma Chaojun, Wu Shangying, and others attended. They discussed and decided on supplementary matters. (A) Regarding the issue of the rights of the people, the following supplementary matters were added: (1) Women shall receive special protection and assistance from the state according to law during and after childbirth and during lactation. (2) The elderly, weak, and disabled people have the right to receive special protection and assistance from the state according to law. (3) The rights of the people of the Republic of China, which are not contrary to the Constitution, shall be recognized. (B) Regarding the issue of the obligations of the people, the following matters were decided: (1) The people have the obligation to perform public service according to law. (3) The people have the obligation to pay taxes according to law. (3) The people have the obligation to perform military service and corvée labor according to law. (4) The people have the obligation to abide by national laws and regulations. (5) The people have the obligation to educate their children. It is reported that the above decisions will be submitted to the sixth meeting of the Constitutional Draft Committee next Thursday for discussion. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Anglo-French Conference Opens the Way for Disarmament Deadlock

MacDonald and Simon Arrive in Paris

Reuters, Geneva, 9th – British Prime Minister MacDonald arrives today. He will meet with French and German representatives, whose views on disarmament are completely contradictory. It will be extremely difficult to find common ground for an agreement. What is most troubling is not only the absence of the US representative to the Disarmament Conference, Davis, but also the absence of any major German officials. During his journey to Geneva, Prime Minister MacDonald spent thirty-six hours in Paris, which has drawn much criticism from the Germans. Today, when Conference President Henderson opened the debate at the General Affairs Committee of the Assembly, he asked all nations to express goodwill towards this important event.

Havas, Paris, 9th – British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon departed from London at 11:00 this morning and arrived in Paris at 5:40 this afternoon. French Premier Daladier and Foreign Minister Pengu personally greeted them at the station. They then accompanied MacDonald and Simon to the British Embassy for an hour-long meeting. Daladier is scheduled to meet with MacDonald and Simon at the State Council at 10:00 tomorrow morning.

TASS, Geneva, 9th – The Political Committee of the Disarmament Conference today resumed discussion of the British disarmament proposal, which suggests that European countries issue a joint declaration formally renouncing the use of force to resolve all international disputes. The committee has decided on a formula that includes the British proposal. The Soviet representative, Dovgalevsky, seized the opportunity to reiterate Litvinov's views expressed last month on revising the British proposal. Dovgalevsky first expressed his support for the Persian representative's proposal to extend the provisions of the declaration to countries outside Europe. He then stated that the Soviet representative firmly opposes dividing countries into two categories, European and non-European, requiring the former not to use force under any circumstances, while the latter only needs to abide by the letter of the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Dovgalevsky said, "Therefore, I fear that this declaration will not only fail to enhance the power of the Kellogg-Briand Pact, but will also diminish it. The Soviet representative is unwilling to join or be responsible for the inevitable tragic consequences of dividing countries into two groups. The Soviet view is that this declaration must be universally extended to all non-European countries in order to be harmless to the Kellogg-Briand Pact and achieve full political effect."

National News Agency, Rome, 9th – Rumors here suggest that Britain has requested Italian Prime Minister Mussolini to personally come to Geneva to assist British Prime Minister MacDonald in making a final effort to save the Disarmament Conference from failure. However, the Italian government has disregarded this request. Authorities claim that the Italian representative to Geneva, Count Aloisi, has been ordered to represent Italy at the Five-Power Talks and will support British Prime Minister MacDonald's effective and constructive proposals to save the Disarmament Conference.

National News Agency, Geneva, 9th – It is rumored that British Prime Minister MacDonald has come to Geneva with a plan to save the Disarmament Conference. British sources here deny this, saying that the Prime Minister is determined to break the deadlock of the conference. As for agreements on establishing air force armaments, military strength, and German equality, concrete proposals will be formulated after meetings in Paris with French cabinet members and in Geneva with representatives from Germany, Italy, and other countries. The Prime Minister is expected to arrive here on Saturday or Sunday and stay for about a week, confident that this trip will be fruitful.

Collapse of the German Federal System

Hitler Seizes Power in Bavaria

Reuters, Berlin, 9th – Hitler's bloodless victory in Bavaria is seen by responsible authorities here as a sign of the collapse of the German federal system. It is now expected that the central government aims to build a unified Germany, with a parliament in Berlin and a central government exercising supreme national authority. The Bavarian government's acceptance of General Epp as administrative commissioner was a painful decision to avoid bloodshed, as the Nazi stormtroopers were armed with pistols and planned to forcibly occupy government offices if the Bavarian government refused. Currently, all government offices, including the parliament, are guarded by armed detachments of Nazi stormtroopers.

National News Agency, Berlin, 9th – Today, the central government appointed General Franz Ritter von Epp, a prominent Nazi Party member, as the administrative commissioner of Bavaria, the last of the federal states to yield. With this, the policy of German unification has been completed. Previously, the Nazi Party leader had held extensive discussions with Bavarian Premier Dr. Held. It is said that Dr. Held initially agreed but then stated that he needed to convene parliament to elect a new premier. Therefore, the central government took decisive measures for the sake of public safety. However, Dr. Held is still protesting. Tonight, Nazi stormtroopers occupied Bavarian government offices, newspaper offices, and radio broadcasting stations. General Epp made a brief speech, announcing his determination to maintain order.

Reuters, Berlin, 10th – The governments of Saxony and Baden have both resigned today. Central representative General Keeling has taken over the administration of Saxony and appointed Nazi Party members to manage various government departments.

Reuters, London, 10th – The occupation of the Strasbourg city hall by Nazi stormtroopers has caused unease in France, as it is seen as a violation of the demilitarized zone. The Berlin party authorities claim that when the stormtroopers acted in Kehl and Karlsruhe, they temporarily occupied the barracks opposite Strasbourg, but have now withdrawn. They also deny violating the Treaty of Versailles, as the barracks were not garrisoned.

Reuters, Berlin, 10th – The famous Berlin Daily News has been ordered by the authorities to cease publication for three days.

Congress Passes Roosevelt's Emergency Law

Major Overhaul of the American Banking System

Only Those with Sufficient Funds Allowed to Operate

President Retains Financial Dictatorial Powers

National News Agency, Washington, 9th – The American banking sector will enter a new era starting tomorrow. Only those with [one hundred percent] solvency will be allowed to operate. Today, the Senate passed an emergency banking bill by a vote of 73 to 7, guaranteeing that banks with solid foundations will have access to sufficient currency for normal business needs. The President has the power to refuse operating licenses to those who cannot prove their solvency. In addition, President Roosevelt is granted dictatorial powers to place the banking system on a stable footing. The bill, after being signed by the President, will take effect at 8:00 tonight. Its contents are as follows:

New Banking Law

(1) All presidential orders and Treasury Department regulations issued before today remain in effect. (2) Reinstates the provisions of the Trading with the Enemy Act, along with the power to prevent hoarding and manage the US gold reserves. (3) Authorizes the President to manage banks to the extent necessary to protect depositors' interests, and authorizes the President and the Treasury Department to quickly reorganize banks with illiquid funds to ensure a solid foundation for permanent liquidity. (4) Amends the Federal Reserve Act, allowing it to directly lend to corporations and individuals using US national debt as collateral, and grants the Federal Reserve Banks broad powers to lend to member banks with solid assets that are currently difficult to use as collateral. It also authorizes the Federal Reserve System to issue Federal Reserve Bank notes, using its own US national debt and notes from corporations, individuals, and partners secured by US national debt as collateral for issuing notes, and may also use notes secured by member banks' solid assets as collateral for issuing notes.

National Support

After the announcement of this bill, there was unanimous support throughout the country. Prominent figures in the financial world explained the significance of the bill, saying that the President will only allow banks with sufficient financial strength to repay debts to reopen. The rest must reduce their assets and reorganize, ensuring that their assets match their actual value before they are allowed to reopen. It is also heard that the President plans to issue a type of operating license, using his newly acquired powers to issue licenses to banks with sufficient solvency. Without a license issued by the federal government, they may not resume normal business. After the bill was passed and signed, it was heard that the New York Clearing House Association would begin clearing checks in preparation for the opening of banks tomorrow. Senator Glass, an expert on finance and banking, also stated that about 64% of the banks under the Federal Reserve System could open on Friday. Senators, cabinet members, and Treasury Department experts all believe that this bill passed by Congress can implement the President's main proposal, which is to allow the issuance of more currency under a plan that does not increase the nation's unsecured debt in the slightest. The gold reserves of the Federal Reserve Banks above the statutory gold reserve ratio, along with

How Many Seek to Harm Roosevelt?

(Reuters, New York, 10th) – The Walter Tang Post Office in New York found a package addressed to the White House. Suspecting it, they opened and inspected it, finding a bomb filled with explosives, clearly intended to harm President Roosevelt. An investigation is underway to find the person who sent the package. On February 22nd, the same post office discovered a similar package addressed to Washington, but fortunately, it was inspected and no disaster occurred.

(National News Agency, Miami, 9th) – Giuseppe Zangara, the assassin who attempted to assassinate President Roosevelt, was previously sentenced to eighty years in prison. Now, due to the death of Chicago Mayor Cermak from his injuries, the court has re-sentenced him to death.

Other legal collateral, is sufficient to provide collateral for a large issuance of new currency.

President's Message

The President's first message to Congress today was only 500 words long, only describing the banking crisis, and can be described as the shortest message on a major crisis. After introducing the current critical situation, the message explicitly told Congress that in order to ensure the stable opening of banks, the President wants broader administrative powers to protect depositors and asks for authorization to stably open banks. As for other banks, once they have achieved a stable foundation, they will be quickly allowed to resume operations. The President believes that this legislation should not only immediately dispel people's unnecessary concerns about very stable banks, but also allow them to start a new relationship between banks and the people. Congress should be deeply aware of the important responsibilities borne by the President and the senators. In this short period of five days, it is impossible to draft a complete plan to avoid the repetition of past mistakes, but the completion of this initial procedure should not be delayed in the slightest. Furthermore, the President will soon ask Congress to formulate two plans, both of which are urgently needed at present. After the implementation of these plans, we can proceed to consider the national recovery plan.

Suspension Extended

National News Agency, Washington, 9th – Roosevelt, in announcing the extension of the bank holiday today, stated that the emergency situation still exists and that it is necessary to issue another announcement extending the amended bank holiday in order to achieve the purpose of the original ban on exports and gold hoarding. During this holiday, gold is not allowed to be moved domestically or exported abroad, nor may ownership of uncoined gold and silver markers be transferred. Foreign exchange speculation will be completely stopped. The banking regulations issued by the Treasury Department will now apply to all banking operations. According to recent reports of gold flowing out of the United States, according to the report released by the Federal Reserve today, gold outflow was very large in the days before the suspension. In the week ending March 8, the United States actually shipped out 7 million yuan in gold, and lost no less than 93,271,000 yuan due to marking ownership of foreign accounts. However, this is still a small number compared to what depositors withdrew domestically. According to the Treasury Department report, the total amount of withdrawals in January and February was only a few yuan short of a whole number of 100 million yuan. If the president had not ordered a ban on movement, the number of withdrawals would have been unknown. Even silver coins are included in the ban during this indefinite suspension period.

Havas, Washington, 10th. Treasury Secretary Woodin issued a

Statement, saying that the purpose of the policy adopted by the Ministry of Finance is to enable sound banks to resume operations immediately whenever possible. After President Roosevelt issued a proclamation on banks, he summoned leaders of the Senate and House of Representatives to a meeting at the White House. During the meeting, the President declared that the procedure adopted by the government was to restore [national life]. After the meeting, a certain important person declared that President Roosevelt intends to issue 50 million gold yuan bonds for afforestation, so as to provide jobs for 50,000 people. Another bill is scheduled to reduce federal government expenditures by 500 million gold yuan, most of which is related to pensions for former war veterans and salaries for civil servants. Roosevelt can submit the budget to the Senate and House of Representatives today.

Havas, New York, 10th - The total of the Federal Reserve Banks for the week ending March 8 shows a decrease of 10.1 million gold yuan in cash deposits, while currency in circulation increased by 81.8 million gold yuan. The amount of spot reserves in the twelve reserve banks has fallen to 45.5 percent. The minimum amount of their statutory reserves is 40 percent.

Reuters, New York, 10th – National hoarders of cash, fearing official punishment, are now sending large amounts of gold coins to banks. The number of deposits yesterday was very large. One person alone paid in 35,000 yuan. It is found that the circulation of gold coins among the people is usually less than 25 million yuan, but during the week before the President ordered the ban on withdrawals, the public scrambled to withdraw cash, resulting in a report from the Federal Reserve Board for the week ending March 8 that the United States' cash reserves decreased by 101,000,000 yuan and the amount of currency in circulation increased by 818,000,000 yuan. Since President Roosevelt issued a warning, hoarders yesterday handed over about 30 million yuan in gold coins in New York alone, for a total of 65 million yuan handed over nationwide.

Expansion of Currency

Reuters, Washington, 9th - The exact amount of U.S. bonds held by U.S. banks is not yet known, but according to private Wall Street estimates, it reached 10,000,000,000 yuan as of March 1. The amount of bank drafts and other notes that can be used as a currency base is currently unknown. It is estimated that the amount currently circulating in the market is 7,250,000,000 yuan. The amount of currency flowing into the United States in February increased by 906,000,000 yuan, reaching a total of 6,546,000,000 yuan. The amount of gold coins in circulation has increased from 47.8837 million yuan to 571.338 million yuan. The number of coins circulating per person nationwide has jumped from 45.06 yuan to 52.23 yuan. This is the highest per capita circulation since the end of October 1920, and the total circulation has reached the highest level on record.

Japanese Influence

Reuters, Tokyo, 10th - To prevent the yen from soaring after the U.S. gold embargo, the Japanese Ministry of Finance today ordered all exchange banks to report the number of yen purchases and sales in accordance with the Law on Preventing the Outflow of Funds. Prices on the Tokyo Stock Exchange rose again today, with various securities rising by two to nine pounds sterling. It is heard that buying is very brisk here after U.S. inflation. The Yokohama Stock Exchange suspended operations after the U.S. announced a bank holiday. It reopened today and the market was calm.

U.S. First Lady Does Not Forget Needlework

(Reuters, Washington, 10th) - The wife of the new President Roosevelt sat in the gallery during the House of Representatives' debate on the bank bill, knitting with knitting needles. When the members of Congress saw her, they all stood up to pay their respects.

Reuters, Tokyo, 10th - The newly appointed Soviet Russian Ambassador to Japan, Yuriniev, arrived in Tsushima this morning. According to his interview with newspaper reporters, negotiating a Russo-Japanese non-aggression treaty is one of his main tasks after taking office in Tokyo.

The Plight of Refugees in the Japanese Earthquake Zone

More Than One Hundred People Die of Hunger and Cold Every Day

Reuters, Tokyo, 10th - This afternoon, the Hochi Shimbun published the plight of refugees in the recent earthquake zone, stating that more than one hundred people are dying of hunger and cold every day, coupled with the prevalence of influenza, with 12,000 patients. Another thousand or so people are suffering from pneumonia.

British Cotton Industry Strives to Regain Foreign Markets

Reuters, London, 10th - The Manchester cotton industry is now launching a plan to raise £2.5 million to form the Lancashire Textiles Cooperative, in order to regain the foreign markets lost by Lancashire cotton goods with lower production costs and improved sales methods. The characteristics of this plan are the direct supply of raw cotton to spinning mills, large-scale wholesale purchases of coal, dyestuffs, etc., centralization of ordering agencies, communication of cotton industry information, and extensive distribution of sales offices around the world.

This is Shaw's first visit to the United States. George Bernard Shaw's wife stayed on the ship due to illness, and only landed yesterday to visit various attractions in Tokyo.

The Strategic Significance of the Japanese Navy's Grand Naval Maneuvers in Japanese Eyes (Continuation 1)

(By Masanori Ito)

Seven, the so-called [Atlantic Fleet]

What has been said above is only a general observation of the current situation and peacetime strategies. If we intend to discuss future strategic directions and tactical significance, we naturally have to observe from other perspectives. Regarding the research on the first phase of the Hawaii offensive and defensive exercises, we have two clues:

(A) Japan's implementation of its strategy in Shanghai and its countermeasures.

(B) The utilization and promotion of the Atlantic Fleet. In addition, what is most evident in the entire exercise is:

(C) Obtaining a portion of air supremacy.

Let us first observe the former two (A and B):

The stipulation that the Hawaiian Islands are occupied by the enemy is a prerequisite for testing future real island occupation battles and joint operations between the army and navy. The attacking force participating in this hypothetical battle is the Atlantic Fleet, which has always attracted much attention. Its composition is as follows:

U.S. Fleet Reconnaissance Force (commonly known as the Atlantic Fleet) flagship Augusta (10,000 tons! 8-inch guns), four squadrons of aviation squadrons,

A. Cruiser Force

Second Cruiser Squadron 丨 Memphis, Milwaukee, Richmond, Trenton (all 7,000 tons, 6-inch guns), eight reconnaissance aircraft,

Fourth Cruiser Squadron 丨 Chester, Northampton, Pensacola (all 10,000-ton heavy cruisers), twelve reconnaissance aircraft,

Fifth Cruiser Squadron 丨 Chicago, Louisville, Salt Lake City, Houston (all 10,000-ton heavy cruisers), twelve reconnaissance aircraft (flagship Chicago, repair ship Vestal)

B. Destroyer Force

Flagship Raleigh, two aviation squadrons, First, Second, Third, Seventh, Eighth, and Ninth Squadrons 丨 a total of twenty-six ships (all 1,200 tons or more oceangoing ships), Nineteenth Reserve Squadron 丨 fifteen ships (medium-sized)

C. Aerial Reconnaissance Force

Flagship Wright (9,553 tons丨27 aircraft), air force guidance ship Langley, Saratoga, Langley (carrying eight to ten aircraft each), eighteen fighter planes (belonging to the flagship), nine reconnaissance planes (same as above), twelve search planes (belonging to the Langley), six for supplementary use (in addition, there are thirty-eight aircraft under the control of the guidance ship Swan)

The above is the total strength of the so-called Atlantic Fleet, which consists of seven heavy cruisers (10,000 tons, 8-inch guns), four 7,000-ton light cruisers, twenty-six first-class destroyers, fifteen second-class destroyers, four aircraft carriers and supply ships, and eighty-three aircraft. The heavy cruisers currently under construction will soon be completed and will also be incorporated into this fleet, while the Second Cruiser Squadron will be incorporated into other fleets. The fleet's great power can already be imagined.

Eight, Rehearsal of the Shanghai Incident

In this exercise, the two major aircraft carriers, Saratoga and Lexington, replaced the air force unit. In terms of cruisers, the light cruisers were removed, and seven 10,000-ton ships were incorporated into the Fourth and Fifth Cruiser Squadrons. The fleet's speed reached more than thirty knots. In terms of the air force, the elite units of the U.S. Navy were mobilized, such as the aircraft carrier Saratoga (33,000 tons, 33 knots) and the Lexington (same tonnage), each carrying thirty-eight fighter planes, twelve reconnaissance planes, eighteen bombers, and ten other aircraft, totaling seventy-eight aircraft per ship. The two ships carried a total of one hundred and fifty-six aircraft. In addition, each cruiser carried four aircraft, totaling twenty-eight aircraft, plus those carried by the directly subordinate supply ships, totaling no less than two hundred and fifty aircraft. This is such a powerful large gathering of aviation squadrons. How about the strength of the enemy forces occupying Hawaii to deal with this counterattack? (A) The air force units of the army and navy, (B) submarines, (C) joint army and navy forces. The force included 111 naval aircraft, 120 army aircraft, one army division, some marines, and the Fourth Squadron of the U.S. submarine force, namely S-class submarines (around 1,000 tons), nineteen ships, and four ships over 2,000 tons (these four ships are oceangoing submarines). Whether by chance or on purpose, the scale of the Hawaii offensive and defensive battle is strikingly similar to the Sino-Japanese war in Shanghai. For example, in (A) using cruisers as the main force, (B) making the marines active, (C) using aircraft to attack fortresses and bombing land and water facilities, etc., (D) having the marines cooperate with the army in combat, are all lifelike depictions of the Shanghai Incident.

Therefore, this exercise can be called a high-level Shanghai Incident in terms of forces and equipment.

Nine, Aerial Tactics

In this plan, what is most noteworthy is that its attacking force is actually the world's unparalleled high-speed air strike force. The following is a summary of its current situation:

Tonnage Cannon Power丨丨Number of Aircraft Speed

Cruiser Squadron 70,000 8-inch guns丨652833

Aviation Battleship 66,000 8-inch guns丨1613633

Torpedo Squadron 15,000 18-inch torpedoes 14435

The fleet's speed reaches thirty-two knots, plus the power of more than 180 air force aircraft. Such a unique naval warfare tactic of quickly attacking enemy countries in wartime can't be said to be an unparalleled ideal organization. With two major aircraft carriers as the center, flanked by seven 10,000-ton cruisers, and protected by twelve destroyers in front and behind, crossing rough seas and dangerous waves, the fleet marches on the Pacific Ocean with magnificence. In essence, such a powerful [high-speed fleet] is unheard of in any other country. Therefore, the tactics of the U.S. naval exercises are unique to the United States.

The high-speed army (Speedy Army) and chemical warfare units are the two major characteristics of the U.S. Army. Now the Navy is also actively trying to realize these two characteristics, and if they want to increase the fleet's combat power, the only way is to improve the fleet's speed at sea and seek rapid attacks. Therefore, the U.S. Navy has decided to use aircraft for attacks, so naval strategy also contains the meaning of air strategy.

The purpose of the Hawaiian attack force's organization is to launch a counterattack when a certain territory or dependency is occupied by the enemy, without waiting for the enemy to complete their defensive arrangements, or to capture a certain target in the shortest possible time after the declaration of war.

Under this strategy, if the enemy forces in Hawaii, whose defensive preparations have not yet been completed, are subjected to the counterattacking forces' bombing and shelling, they will surrender after a major air battle. (February 5) When the U.S. flag is re-hoisted in Hawaii, the enemy fleet will begin its offensive towards the Pacific Ocean. (February 6)

Ten, Submarines

During this battle, the spectacle and power of the thirty-six bombers of the attacking force flying in the air over Oahu Island during the attack was many times stronger than that of our (Japanese) air force bombing the Wusong Fort. When the Hawaiian defense forces were attacking the enemy with dozens of fighter planes in the air, the attacking force launched seventy-six fighter planes in a counterattack. At this time, the lightly armed reconnaissance planes also joined in. There were no less than two hundred aircraft flying in the sky like leaves. The spectacle must have been beyond imagination. However, what effect did submarines have on defense at this time? Hawaii had twenty-five submarines. The big target of these ships' attack was the two major aircraft carriers, Saratoga and Lexington. The defense force relied on submarines to launch torpedoes and attack the enemy's aircraft carriers. If one of the two ships could be sunk, the enemy's air control power would be halved, which would not only comfort the residents' fear of air raids, but also greatly aid the main artillery battle in modern naval warfare. Whether the Hawaiian submarine fleet can achieve the above expectations, we can only wait for the battle reports of future exercises. In addition, one thing that is extremely noteworthy is that there are no submarines in the attacking force, and there are no submarines in the organization of the U.S. Navy's main fleet.

Looking at the attacking force in this Hawaii battle, they attach great importance to the aircraft carrier group (Carrier Group), but they don't have a single submarine. This is an indication that submarines are not used in offensive warfare. In other words, submarines are only used for coastal defense and not for offensive attacks. The difference between Japan and the United States (and Britain) in the evaluation of submarines can be seen from this.

What is even more noteworthy is the reason why the attacking force does not use submarines, which is instead convenient for main force operations. There are two meanings to this reason: one is that torpedoes can be launched from the air, and the other is that the enemy's submarines can be bombed from the air. The U.S. Navy's use of the air force is the best in the world, and their technology for bombing enemy submarines discovered in the air cannot be ranked second in the world. The reason why the U.S. attacking force does not use submarines is that if they also have submarines, it would be difficult for the air force to distinguish between enemy and friendly submarines during reconnaissance, causing the greatest difficulty in tactics. Therefore, if a submarine is discovered in the air, it must be the enemy and can be safely bombed.

This is one of the things that naval countries that value submarines in peacetime pay the most attention to. At the same time, the reason why the attacking force did not use submarines in this exercise can also be understood from this.

Eleven, Attack on the West Coast

In the second phase of the exercise, the reconnaissance force that recaptured Hawaii, consisting of heavy cruisers and aircraft carriers, immediately turned its bow and began an invasion of the U.S. mainland after the Hawaii battle. Defending the U.S. mainland was the Pacific Fleet, the main battleship fleet, consisting of fourteen battleships, four cruisers, thirty-five destroyers, and several aviation squadrons. During the period from February 6 to February 17, the purpose of this exercise announced by the U.S. authorities was to [maximize the test of the U.S. West Coast's defense capabilities] in response to the rapid attack of the rapid attack force and to defend the national coast. From this point of view, this second phase of the exercise, the occupation of the base exercise, is the most important of the three exercises. Using the main battle force as the defending force is not only an indication of taking a defensive exercise, but also somewhat intended to test and promote the large cruisers participating in this attacking force, and the testing and promotion of aviation power is also its secondary purpose.

The first thing that unfolds in this exercise is the naval battle between the attacking and defending forces. The second is that the attacking force invades any one of the three places: San Francisco, San Diego, and San Pedro. In this place, joint army and navy battles, air battles, etc., are re-enacted. The bombers of the Saratoga and Lexington bombed the U.S. West Coast's military equipment, fortresses, bases, factories, etc. The defending fighter planes engaged in interception. On the one hand, the army and navy exchanged artillery fire. At this time, the incompleteness of land equipment and the uneven strength of the water fleet are naturally clear to the people.

Twelve, Joint Training and Chemical Warfare

The third phase of the exercise is a full-scale exercise of the U.S. fleet, including (1) joint tactical exercises, (2) artillery fire, and (3) torpedo firing training, held from March 5th to approximately twenty days, and (4) combat skills demonstration on March 31st. During this period, new types of shooting such as [colored water columns] and [remote illumination] were also demonstrated. Colored water columns are the water columns raised when the main gun shells of each ship fall into the water near the enemy ship. Because of the different ships, they are dyed various colors. For example, the USS Colorado is red and the USS Maryland is yellow. Each ship has its own distinguishing color, so that the aircraft can measure the distance between the falling shells and the enemy ship from the air and report it to the firing ship to seek accurate aiming. Firing one or two shots at an enemy more than 30,000 yards away will not hit the target. First, observe the first shot falling dozens of yards in front of the enemy, then aim the second shot and fire it, watching it fall dozens of yards behind the enemy, and then aim the third shot and fire it into the bullseye. Therefore, the shells falling into the water at the same time from each ship can be measured for distance due to the different ships, which is of course thanks to the [colored water column].

Although illumination shells are nothing strange, when fired from a battleship's giant guns and explode fifteen miles above the enemy ship, they can suddenly illuminate the surroundings of a diameter of 500 yards, and then attack it with artillery. This kind of demonstration is deeply meaningful. The U.S. Navy's efforts in the development of chemical warfare are also worthy of surprise.

Torpedoes are very important in the Japanese Navy, but the opposite is true in the United States. The center of combat skills in joint training is mainly the aviation squadron. If torpedoes are launched from warships, they suffer from direction errors and speed errors, making them difficult to be accurate. Moreover, at a distance of 30,000 yards, the hit rate and effect must be reduced. Therefore, some people advocate that in the future, they should be launched from aircraft, that is, when the enemy's fighter planes cannot descend and within the distance where the enemy ship fires the least number of times, torpedoes can be launched from the aircraft. The effect is of course greater than being launched from a warship. Finally, write two important conclusions. (To be continued)

Li Liejun's Visit to Bing

Discussing Anti-Japanese Plans with Yan

Taiyuan Correspondence: It was reported from the Sui Pacification Headquarters the day before yesterday that Central Committee members Li Liejun, Chuan Rulin, and Zhao Pilian were scheduled to arrive in Bing together on the 6th. The deputy director of the Public Relations Department, Xue Chongxue, was dispatched to Shijiazhuang to welcome them. After Chuan and Zhao arrived in Shijiazhuang, they transferred to Xinxiang and were scheduled to come to Bing again in two or three days. Li Liejun then transferred to the Zhengtai express train and arrived in Bing at 4:00 PM yesterday. The official side pre-sent one platoon each of police and military police, and a military band to welcome and guard the station. At around 3:00 PM, Sun Chu, the commander of the Railway Protection Command, Rong Honglu, the commander of the Garrison Command, Li Shengda, the commander of the 72nd Division, Li Runfa, the commander of the Military Police, Zhao Daiwen, the chief of staff, Hu Zhushouguang, Xu Yongchang, the chairman of the Provincial Government, and the directors of the relevant departments, Guo Maozhi, the director of the Public Relations Department, Wang Xifu, the director of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, and others went to the station. Sui Pacification Director Yan Xishan went to the station in a special car at the last moment. Less than ten minutes after arriving at the station, the train whistle blew loudly. All the welcomers at the station stood up silently upon hearing the whistle. Soon the train arrived, and the military band immediately played music. Commissioner Li got off the train amid the welcoming sounds. Yan and Zhao both stepped forward to greet him. Li smiled and nodded in return. After being introduced by the personnel from the Public Relations Department, Li expressed his gratitude one by one. Then he walked and talked with Yan, Zhao, and others, and went straight to the Shanxi Grand Hotel to rest. Yan and Li talked for about ten minutes at the hotel and then bid farewell and returned to the headquarters. Li stayed in Room 14 on the second floor of the hotel. However, the news of Feng's arrival in Bing has not been confirmed as of yesterday. At 6:00 PM yesterday evening, a reception was held at the Sui Pacification Headquarters to welcome Li. Important figures from military and political circles attended. It is said that Li's visit to Bing this time is to discuss major plans against Japan with Yan. (March 7)

Residents Gather at the Consulate

Wuhu Correspondence: After the Japanese Consul in Wuhu, Shirasaki Hakubo, requested protection for Japanese residents from Gao Tiejun, the administrative commissioner of the Second District and concurrently the county magistrate of Wuhu, the Japanese warships stationed in Wuhu suddenly increased. As of yesterday (the 8th), there were already three ships, Taohaji, Yanagi, and Flying Eagle, stationed on the river surface near the Osaka pier and Taikoo wharf. It is said that there are two more ships parked in the Crab Creek area downstream. The bows of all the ships point directly at Wuhu, and Japanese soldiers and residents are constantly active everywhere, causing the people of Wuhu to have a strange feeling. Our navy also has two ships, Jiankang and Qingtian, stationed outside the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company wharf. The British ships HMS Scarboro and HMS P were here yesterday. This morning, HMS P already weighed anchor and sailed downstream. According to investigations, there are thirteen male and female staff members of the Japanese Consulate and Japanese Police Department in the Japanese Consulate in Wuhu, including businessmen such as Sato Izumi, a rice broker, Erigo Jiro, an egg dealer, Yoneda Yoshimi and Hosokawa Sakae of the Shiooka Yoko, Kiyata Tatsujiro, Hama Naga Miiichi of the Japanese Elementary School, Nitta Shuichi, Binta of the Nitta Ryokan, Hayashi Masashige of the Japanese Club, and Mitsubishi Company and NYK Line, totaling about thirty men and women. Fuzhou's Movement to Resist Inferior Goods and Buy Aircraft

Organizing Donation Teams to Raise Funds to Purchase Aircraft

Prohibiting the Enemy from Smuggling Raw Materials to Taiwan

Fuzhou Correspondence: The people of Minyuan had previously initiated the organization of the Minhou Aviation Patriotic Association and elected Sa Zhenbing as the chairman. They originally planned to issue lottery tickets to use the profits earned to purchase aircraft. Later, because the provincial government considered lottery tickets to be a form of gambling, it was not allowed to issue them. Yesterday, the association decided to organize forty-six donation teams to set out to solicit donations separately. The method is to have the thirty-four fire brigades in the city organize thirty-four teams, and the twelve autonomous regions organize twelve teams. The association will send people to assist in the process. At the same time, all members of the association will also organize special teams to solicit donations from party, government, and military agencies in order to realize the purchase of aircraft to save the country as soon as possible.

The Provincial Capital People's Patriotic Association has recently suspended its work due to lack of funds, causing unscrupulous merchants to become active again and inferior goods to flood the market, especially the silk, Suzhou and Guangdong goods, hardware, seafood, coal, white sugar, and Western medicine industries. Every time Japanese ships imported from Taiwan and Dalian are fully loaded with goods and carry timber and white rice away. This is hateful to destroy the economy, sever diplomatic relations, and provide raw materials to the enemy. Yesterday, a meeting of all personnel was convened to decide to conduct a general inspection in the coming days. If inferior goods are found again in stores that have previously registered with the Patriotic Association and been cleaned up, they will be confiscated and sold at auction, used as funds for the volunteer army, or used to purchase aircraft. It was also decided to severely punish those who smuggle timber and white rice to Dalian and Taiwan. (March 7)

Guangxi Province Actively Expands Aviation

Building a Huge Airfield

Adding Six Fighter Planes

Wuzhou Correspondence: Guangxi Province has recently been quite active in developing its aviation industry, carrying out pilot training and increasing the purchase of aircraft separately. The Aviation Office is currently located in Liushi, and the airfield is extremely vast. The hangars are located in underground cellars to protect the storage of aircraft. The area around the hangars is covered with defensive works, and the layout is extremely strict. The entire airfield project is still under construction and is divided into three phases, each phase lasting four months. The entire project will be completed in about one year. The first phase of the project requires 600 workers, so the scale is very large. In terms of training personnel, training classes were initially organized to train individual flight personnel. The first phase recruited 60 students, divided into three teams, with a total of eleven pilots and mechanics in each team. One instructor is responsible for training one team. It has been operating for six months, and 22 students are now familiar with solo flight. The skills of the mechanics have also been quite successful. The instructors are all hired from Guangdong. The current instructors include Zheng Zixiang, Guo Liangbi, and Situ Kai. Bishop Situ Kai died in a flight accident last month, and pilot Chen Youshou from Guangdong was hired to fill the vacancy. Last year, Ning Mingjie, Wu Zihong, Li Yifei and others were re-hired as instructors. The first phase of the training class, with 22 pilots, will soon graduate. They are already familiar with solo flight and squadron flight, so the Aviation Office is now holding the second phase of the training class and increasing the training in attack, pursuit, bombing, and reconnaissance techniques. Guangxi Province currently has 20 fighter planes and several training planes in storage. For the sake of expansion, a large number of aircraft supplies and six fighter planes have been purchased from the Far East Aviation Company in Hong Kong and have been shipped to Hong Kong. Zheng Zixiang, representative of the Guangxi Aviation Office, was sent to Hong Kong to inspect the planes. Ning Mingjie, Wu Zihong, and Li Yifei were sent to Wuzhou to wait for the delivery. Zheng visited Li Zongren in Guangdong at the end of last month and reported everything. On the 2nd of this month, he went to the Far East Company in Hong Kong to carry out the inspection. It is planned to ship four fighter planes back to Wuzhou on the 6th. Four foreign pilots from the Far East Company will take off from the Kai Tak Airport in Kowloon and fly to Wuzhou. The remaining two planes are scheduled to be driven back to Guangxi by Zheng himself and the pilots on the 8th. As for the aircraft supplies, they will be transported back to Wuzhou by water and then transported to Liu by land. (March 5)

Nanjing Yunjian Fellow-Villagers Association Construction Report

Beijing News: Fellow villagers from the seven counties of Songjiang have recently formed the Yunjian Traveling Beijing Fellow-Villagers Association and have launched a fundraising campaign. Construction is now underway. However, due to the impact of floods and the invasion of the violent Japanese, the national crisis is imminent, and it is not easy to raise funds. It has been postponed repeatedly. As of the end of February this year, we have received donations of 9,893 yuan, plus 465 yuan under the old management, totaling 10,358 yuan. After deducting 4,073 yuan for the purchase of the base and road construction fees, there is actually a balance of 6,285 yuan. There are also about 3,000 yuan that have been pledged but not yet paid, and more than ten teams that have not yet reported. We are now building the rear five upper and five lower, including the lower rooms, etc., which will cost about 8,500 yuan. We have already paid 5,500 yuan. It is expected to be completed by the end of May. Once completed, we will hold a general meeting of all members at the new clubhouse at a fixed time. At that time, we will print and distribute the list of donors. As for the remaining two courtyards, we can only decide based on the amount of continued donations. Sincerely, the Executive and Supervisory Committee Members of the Yunjian Traveling Beijing Fellow-Villagers Association."

Currently, workers are hired to build embankments to create an irrigation experimental field.

After questioning by Prosecutor Wang, he was sent to the detention center.

The staff of the Nantong County Property Office resigned due to the expiration of their terms. The county government is currently reorganizing the office, deciding to appoint Wu Xuxian, Liu Shiru, and Zhao Shouyong as the director and deputy directors. Wu and others declined, but the county government persuaded them to stay on the 9th.

Ningbo

Establishment of a Cooperative for the Transportation and Sale of Fritillaria Bulbs

The Zhangcun area in western Yin County produces over 800,000 catties of fritillaria bulbs annually, worth tens of thousands of dollars. Over ten thousand households depend on this for their livelihood. Last year, Zheng Jiahao and others in the industry initiated the establishment of the Zhejiang Limited Liability Fritillaria Bulb Transportation and Sales Cooperative. Over four thousand people joined the cooperative. Its scale is among the largest cooperative enterprises in Yin County, and it can be considered a leading example. It is now learned that the cooperative has been prepared and held its inaugural meeting yesterday at the Wenchang Pavilion in Zhangcun. Representatives from the Provincial Department of Construction and the County Government were sent to the meeting for guidance. Over a thousand representatives from all walks of life, members, and guests attended the meeting, which was quite grand for a time. After holding the inauguration ceremony, the first general meeting of cooperative members was held at 7:00 PM to discuss the cooperative's charter and elect directors, economic committee members, and evaluation committee members.

Local News

Silver Dollar Standard Implemented Yesterday

The Exchange Management Committee is Busy

New Currency Issued, Old Currency Still Usable

Customs Duty Collection Also Changed to Silver Dollar Calculation

Starting yesterday, all industries in this city implemented the silver dollar standard. From now on, transactions are calculated in silver dollars. Silver and copper exchange businesses have abolished foreign exchange rates. The Exchange Management Committee, jointly established by the three banks, has started working. The new currency has already been circulated in the market. Details are as follows:

Suspension of Foreign Exchange

The Ningbo Road money exchange market announced yesterday the resolution of the Money Exchange Association to suspend foreign exchange rates and change the silver discount to discount interest. Morning and afternoon markets gather and trade as usual. The exchange rate is calculated according to the legal rate of 7 qian, 1 fen, and 5 li. All shops and businesses, both internally and externally, comply with the resolution of the association.

Abolition of Exchange Rates

The exchange rate committee organized by various banks, in accordance with the instructions of the Ministry of Finance, has used the silver standard to calculate all prices and exchange rates since yesterday. Therefore, the silver exchange rate boards for Hankou, Tianjin, and other places that were previously displayed daily have been abolished. All banks' remittances to Tianjin and Hankou are based on silver dollars. Furthermore, banks' foreign exchange has also been changed to be calculated in silver dollars.

All Industries Comply

All industries were notified by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce that, starting yesterday, all transactions and other items should be converted to silver dollar calculations at the legal rate of 7 qian, 1 fen, and 5 li. Foreign banks' transactions with Chinese businesses are also converted to silver dollars at the legal rate. Although north-south remittance houses still allow the issuance of silver notes when customers need them, the majority of bank notes issued yesterday were in silver dollars.

Exchange Committee in Office

The Shanghai Silver Dollar and Silver Taels Exchange Management Committee, jointly established by the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications, upon the order of the Ministry of Finance, began working at 9:00 AM yesterday in the Cash Department of the Central Bank's Business Bureau. Exchanges by money exchange houses are handled by the Money Exchange Joint Reserve. A total of over 1.2 million yuan was exchanged from taels to dollars or from dollars to taels, making the Management Committee's work very busy. All followed the regulations, first filling out a request form, stating the purpose, and closing at 2:00 PM. After approval, account transfers or designated bank withdrawals began at 3:00 PM.

New Currency Issued

The Central Mint was ordered on March 1st to mint new currency with the portrait of Sun Yat-sen. The new currency minted daily is managed by the Exchange Management Committee, jointly established by the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications. It began circulating in the market yesterday. Various money exchange houses and banks have received it, but the number issued is not large. As for the old currency in the market, it is still used as usual.

Customs Notice

Tang Haian, the Superintendent of the Jianghai Customs, and Tax Commissioner Bode, jointly issued Notice No. 1282 yesterday regarding the change to the calculation of various import and export taxes and transit surcharges using the new silver currency. The notice stated that, according to the government's order, starting from March 10th of this year, Customs Taels will be abolished and replaced with newly minted silver currency. This silver currency has a fineness of 88 and contains 23.493448 grams of pure silver. The conversion rate for Customs Taels is set at 7 qian, 1 fen, and 5 li. One hundred Customs Taels is equivalent to 155.80 yuan of the newly minted silver standard currency. From this date, all export taxes, transit taxes, surcharges, and various levies that were previously collected in Customs Taels will be calculated using this new currency. The value of local goods used for statistics will also be clearly stated using the newly minted silver standard currency. Before this new silver currency is widely circulated, existing silver dollars circulating locally that have the same value as the silver dollars with Sun Yat-sen's portrait will continue to be accepted as the new silver standard currency. Other types of silver dollars will be accepted at market prices. However, import taxes and other taxes collected in gold units will still be handled as before. Therefore, it should be complied with immediately, and all merchants should be informed.

Heavy Bushel Crisis Resolved

Ship Merchants Resume Shipping Unanimously Today

Flat Bushel Funnel Decided After Inspection

Temporary Strike Joint Association Ends

The Da Gong News reported that the ship merchant heavy bushel strike crisis was resolved yesterday after the second inspection by party and government agencies at Rengu Hall. It was decided to adopt the flat bushel funnel. Before all ship merchants have prepared funnels, a transitional period of one month is tentatively set. The bushel division will still use flat bushels. Ship merchants of all factions will resume shipping unanimously today. The strike joint association will be closed. The details are as follows:

Inspection Decision

Yesterday at one o'clock in the afternoon, the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Bureau of Social Affairs held the second inspection of Jingqi at Rengu Hall on Zhonghua Road. Over sixty representatives from various rice industry organizations and ship merchants attended (representatives from rice shops were absent). The Inspection Office inspected the leaky bushel, zuba, and two-ba bucket three times in succession. The statistics showed that the quantity measured by the flat bushel funnel was accurate, so it was decided to adopt it.

Joint Notice

Party and government agencies jointly notified the North and South City Ship Merchant Lianyi Association to inform the ship merchants to resume shipping immediately. The original text stated: "This is a notice regarding the dispute over bushels of rice. The party and government agencies have now determined the standards and implementation methods. Before these standards and methods are implemented, a transitional period of one month is tentatively set. The bushel division will still use flat bushels. In addition to the party and government agencies sending personnel to the North and South Rice Markets at any time to supervise the bushels, the association should inform the rice boats to resume shipping immediately. If disputes arise during the busheling of rice, direct conflict and disturbances are not allowed. This is extremely important. This is especially notified. Jiang Huaisu, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters; Zhang Binghui, representative of the Bureau of Social Affairs."

Notice of Resumption of Shipping

After receiving the joint notice from party and government agencies, the North and South City Rice Merchants Lianyi Association jointly issued a notice on the same night, stating that shipping would resume unanimously today, and the backlog of goods would be sorted out. Ding Genhe, Wu Fuhai, Lu Junwen, Jin Weixiang, Zhang Fusheng, and five others were sent to Huangdu and Minhang to notify empty boats to return to the mainland for loading. Rice boats that had arrived in Shanghai to unload were also notified by telegram by the association last night.

Joint Association Ends

When the ship merchants declared a strike, the strike joint association was established to seek unified organization and concentrated strength. Now that the heavy bushel crisis has been resolved, Chen Zhiqiang, the chief representative of the association, notified all departments to handle the closure within two days for reporting and collection.

As soon as the troops arrived in Chosun, they suddenly encountered an invasion by 4,000 Japanese soldiers Suzuki, and puppet Wang Jiaju, etc. At that time, Dong brigade was guarding Chaoyang. Rear is Empty

From Chengde to Fuxin and Kailu, there are 1,200 li. Fuxin, which is between Kai and Zhao, was garrisoned by the enemy army (Feng Zhanhai's Department). Since the puppet Allied Army attacked us, our rear was a distant 1,200 li, with no defense forces, no military stations, no supplies, and no rations. All guns and bullets were supplied by Chengde, and all food and drink had to be sought out on our own. How inconvenient it was!

Tang's Younger Brother's Revolt

Tang Yulin's younger brother wanted to obtain a certain-level military officer position in Dong's brigade, which incited the anger of the regiment of the brigade, so they rebelled and defected. Once Chaoyang was lost, the entire situation was shaken. Our army could have retreated from Fuxin to Jianping, but the rebel troops led the rebel army to occupy Jianping. Our army then concentrated on Chifeng, and then concentrated on Chifeng from Xiawazi and Daxintala. At that time, Sun Dianying's army also reinforced Chifeng from the hunting ground. Unfortunately, misunderstandings arose again, which is extremely regrettable.
