Aviation Association Informs the Nation That Consolidating Air Defense Is the Beginning of Relieving National Crisis

If We Abandon Ourselves, the Calamity of Chengde Will Spread Throughout the Country

The Nation Relies on Air Defense; the Lessons from the Three Northeastern Provinces and Rehe Are Not Far Off

The Public Should Spontaneously Organize; Every Drop of Contributions Should Be Used

Since the fall of Chengde, some people have expressed despair over national affairs due to indignation, and some have suspected that the movement to save the country through aviation is too slow to remedy the current difficulties. The China Aviation Association specially issued a declaration this morning, stating the importance of air defense, and urging the people of the country to take the fall of Rehe as a warning and work harder. The original text is recorded as follows:

A Letter from the Aviation Association to the People of the Country: Since the establishment of this association, all parties have placed high expectations on it, and the whole country has given assistance. Although the recruitment of members lasted no more than ten days, the results have been remarkable. We are deeply gratified. However, with the fall of Chengde and the danger to North China, a few passionate people, gambling that one or two cowardly divisions and fleeing generals would lightly abandon the country and shame the international community, have tended to fall into the abyss of despair, thinking that national affairs are like this, and they should live in solitude to the end. Alas, filling ourselves with a self-abandoning mentality is enough to erode the nation's vitality, and is it the wish of our patriotic people to be ruined from now on? But how did Rehe fall? It is right to say that it was due to the cowardice of the commander, the lack of preparation, the inconvenience of transportation, and the obstruction of communication. However, if we think calmly, we will know that the enemy's military strength is far superior to ours. We only rely on ancient organizational methods, while the enemy is rich in modern weapons. We only rely on the bravery of the army, while the enemy uses the power of the air force to control the fate of our army. Leaving aside other things, the enemy planes speeding across towering mountains and ridges, scouting our military situation, destroying our positions, slaughtering our compatriots, and demoralizing us, isn't the enemy's rampant destruction enough to make our loyal and brave soldiers toil in vain and end up drinking their hatred? Alas, if our people witness the fall of Chengde and become despondent from now on, no longer eagerly donating to support our aviation national defense, then the calamity of Chengde will follow and spread throughout the country. Thinking of this, how can we not tremble with fear? It is not just a matter of dealing with the temporary national crisis. We are born in this world, and since we cannot be without a country, the country cannot be without defense. And air defense is the latest and most effective weapon of national defense and the most effective means of self-defense. We cannot be without a country for a single day, so we cannot be without air defense for a single day. The lack of organization in air defense in the past has already caused us to lose three provinces and fall into Rehe. If we are still a nation without air resistance today, can our people's lives and our country's vitality be permanently secured from now on? This is a serious question that we hope our compatriots across the country will deeply consider. This association was organized in response to the painful events in Shanghai, and now the recruitment of members coincides with the fall of the Northeast and the fall of Chengde. Thinking of the national crisis, we feel even more inspired. Now that the whole country is filled with grief and indignation, and the army is full of soldiers who can fight, if we can unite as one and save the country through aviation, with everyone joining this association as members, then the day when the foundation of aviation national defense is consolidated will also be the day when the unprecedented national crisis is relieved. Time waits for no one; let us rise up together. Finally, this association has something more to say: This association is a spontaneous organization of the people. Although the government appreciates its aspirations and has appointed directors and supervisors, the association's affairs are conducted independently, and the membership fees collected are issued by the association. After collection, the association's management committee is responsible for the safekeeping, and the management committee is composed of the association's directors and celebrities from all walks of life. In the future, how the association will use the funds, how it will develop its business, and how it will contribute to the government will all be decided by the association based on public opinion. The government has no intention of interfering, and the benefits of every drop of contribution going to the public are beyond doubt. People from all walks of life are requested to take note.

The Director of the Bureau of Public Works Receives the Architectural Community: Shen Yi, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Public Works in this city, was invited by Wu Tiecheng, the leader of the Shanghai Recruitment Team of the China Aviation Association, to serve as the captain of Team 270. Therefore, on the 8th of this month, he held a tea party at the YMCA for people in the architectural community in this city. The attendees included Fan Wenzhao, Zhao Shen, Li Hongru, Qi Minghe, Tang Wenti, Gu Daosheng, Zheng Hanxi, Yao Changan, Geng Guangzong, Li Keng, Du Ruiji, Li Pan, Lu Qianshou, Lian Jun, Xu Zhitian, Li Zufan, Zhu Shuyi, Jin Tongyin, Wu Zhenying, Su Xiaxuan, Huang Yuanji, Yang Runyu, Huang Ziqiang, Miao Kaibo, Zhou Lexi, Guan Songsheng, and others, totaling twenty-six people. Director Shen delivered a speech on the important significance of saving the country through aviation, and decided to form sub-teams for the convenience of recruitment. As a result, all attendees enthusiastically participated and took on the roles of sub-team leaders to carry out recruitment. The architects who were unable to attend due to other commitments also inquired about the methods by telephone afterwards and expressed their willingness to provide support, which is sufficient to prove the enthusiasm of the community for the aviation national salvation movement.

The Local Court Has Deducted Donations from Salaries: The Central Political Conference resolved to donate funds for saving-the-nation airplanes and ordered all courts and departments to comply accordingly. The Shanghai Local Court has now received an order from the Jiangsu Higher Court, which was forwarded by the Ministry, that all officials, clerks, police officers, and servants should have their salaries deducted according to the standard and remitted. It is reported that the minimum donation must be more than two months' salary. The President, the Chief Prosecutor, and others have already issued orders to all subordinates to comply.

Kong Xiangxi Speaks on the Economic Situation in Europe and America

The Industrial and Commercial Management Association Held a Luncheon Banquet Yesterday

The World's Industry Is Worthy of Our Reference

The Causes of the Economic Panic Are Extravagance and Speculation

Our Country Should Control the Economy, Harmonize Labor and Management, and Revitalize Agriculture

The China Industrial and Commercial Management Association held a luncheon discussion meeting at the Lianhua General Assembly on Beijing Road at 12:00 noon yesterday, and at the same time, it held a banquet for Mr. Kong Xiangxi, who had just returned from abroad after inspecting industries. Mr. Kong is the chairman of the association, so the association also invited him to speak on his experience and feelings from this industrial inspection, so that the industrial and commercial circles of this port can understand the industrial situation abroad and learn from it. The attendees included Pan Xulun, Pan Yangyao, Chen Jicheng, He Dekui, Zhang Zilian, Chen Liting, Wu YunChu, Li Zhaohuan, Cao Xuexiang, Xu Yongzuo, Li Zufan, Mu Jiechu, Liu Hongsheng, Zhao Jinqing, Fang Yixian, and former Minister of Industry Kong Xiangxi, totaling more than 40 people. Mr. Kong gave a speech on his feelings about this overseas industrial inspection and his opinions on the future development of industry in China. After the speech, He Dekui, Li Gongpu, and others asked questions one after another, and Mr. Kong answered them one by one. The meeting ended at 2:00 p.m. The following is a record of Mr. Kong's speech and answers:

Eliminating Evils and Preserving Benefits: Mr. Kong stood up and gave a speech, first briefly describing the international relations and status of our country today, and taking concerted efforts as the key. Then, he spoke about his observations and feelings from this inspection. He said, "I went abroad to inspect industries at a time when the world was experiencing an economic panic and industrial decline. When I arrived in the United States, someone said to me, 'Your trip is not well-timed. I am afraid you will not be able to see the prosperity of this industry.' My intention is exactly the opposite. If we only see the economic prosperity of advanced countries, we will take the system of prosperous countries as our teacher without knowing its drawbacks. Now that it is tending towards decline, it is enough for us to learn from it, so that the construction of our country can preserve its benefits and eliminate its evils, just as a doctor can prescribe a treatment after seeing the symptoms."

Serious Unemployment: The total population of the United States is 120 million, and the number of regularly unemployed people is more than 14 million. If the wives and children of the unemployed are included, there are at least 40 million, accounting for one-third of the country's population. The seriousness of the problem can be seen. Thousands of banks have collapsed in a year, and the social and economic panic has reached its extreme. When I was in New York, someone led me to see the vault of a bank and said, "These are all banknotes." Because depositors feared that banks would collapse, they withdrew their deposits and stored them in vaults, causing social finance to stagnate and fall into panic every day.

Excessive Enjoyment: The situation of unemployment and panic in European countries such as Germany and England is similar. The reasons are nothing more than two: First, excessive consumption during peacetime. Before the panic occurred, workers' lives were relatively stable. They paid attention to enjoyment. Coupled with the relationship of mass production and the method of promotion, they tried to benefit customers. By paying ten yuan first, you can get a car, and five yuan can buy a piano. The rest is gradually paid from the weekly wages. Once unemployed, there is no fixed income, so of course they cannot afford to pay. The items used in the past are all recovered, even the beds and chairs needed for daily use are donated to pay off debts. Tens of thousands of people are wandering the streets all day long without a home to return to in New York City alone. Mass Speculation: The second reason is speculation. Larger companies sell their stocks on the market, and many investors engage in this type of trading, using the rise and fall of prices to seek profits. The rise and fall of stocks depend entirely on the supply and demand of the market, and no one asks about the prosperity or decline of the company. Moreover, due to overproduction, production is suspended, and stock prices plummet. Some stocks are worth 500 yuan, but the selling price is less than 5 yuan. Bankruptcies follow one another, and everyone is implicated, so the social economy becomes more and more panic. The situation in France is slightly different. Because it does not have large industries, but produces small industries, there is no such panic. Italians often say that we are not as rich as the United States, so we have not suffered the crisis of the United States.

Tariff Barriers: Today, the most problematic issue in European and American countries is war debts. European countries owe a lot of debts during the war, and in recent years, all countries have fallen into economic panic. They do not have huge amounts of money to pay off their debts, and can only pay them off with goods. However, the goods produced by the United States themselves cannot be sold well, so why do they need goods from other countries to offset them? Therefore, tariff barriers are becoming higher and higher, causing international trade to shrink day by day, and the flow of finance is also becoming narrower, and the world economic panic is becoming more and more critical. However, the United States cannot abandon war debts, because they were raised from the people at the time of fundraising, and now the people are in poverty and panic, so how dare the government decisively exempt them to increase the burden on the people?

Five Opinions: The results of my trip to the world have provided many lessons for the future development of industry in our country, which should be followed by us. In short, there are about five points: 1. The government and important industrial and commercial groups should have considerable economic control over the national industry. 2. Strive to make the production volume and consumption volume compatible. 3. Prevent excessive expansion of speculative undertakings. 4. Strive for the coordination of labor and management. 5. Promote and revitalize agriculture, so that our country's collapsed economy can have hope of recovery, and lay a solid foundation for the development of industry and commerce.

The Situation in France: After Mr. Kong's speech, He Dekui asked about the economic situation in France. Mr. Kong replied that it was relatively good. People always regard Paris as representing France, which is a big mistake, because Paris is an international playground, and all its facilities are designed to attract tourists from other countries, not the true colors of France. The French are very diligent and good at saving, so the domestic economy is relatively stable. Then someone asked about Britain's attitude towards the Sino-Japanese dispute. Mr. Kong replied that the British do not want to be a third-party sacrifice and try to avoid getting involved in the vortex.

Social Revolution: Finally, Li Gongpu asked whether the economic panic in the United States, Germany, and Britain is becoming more and more serious. In contrast to the economic construction in the Soviet Union, is it about to erupt into a social revolution? Mr. Kong replied that the British economy has begun to show an upward trend. Germany must depend on whether Hitler can change his attitude after taking office. He is afraid that too much high pressure will cause repercussions. The situation in the United States is the most complicated and difficult to predict. However, Americans are full of self-confidence and responsibility, and may be able to work hard to overcome this difficulty.

Two Organizations Write to the Chamber of Commerce to Pay Attention to Inferior Goods Being Passed Off as National Goods

Examine the Production and Sales Volume at Any Time

The Nanjing Road Business Association and the First District Branch of the Citizens Association jointly wrote to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday, asking them to pay attention to inferior goods being passed off as national goods. The original letter stated, "Dear Sirs, according to the discussion at the general meeting of our association members [on how to determine the method of saving the country and earnestly carry it out], the majority of the members present proposed that recently, some national goods manufacturers have been using the certificates of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce and national goods organizations to secretly pass off inferior goods and replace trademarks to pass off as national goods, especially dyeing and printing factories and cotton yarn merchants. Germany Will Change Its National Flag

German僑在本市 Inclined to the Old National Flag

The "North China Daily News" reported that whether Germany will still use the black, red, and gold tricolor flag as the national flag, or change to the old black, white, and red tricolor flag, is a problem that Germany will solve. The German expatriates in this port are calmly dealing with it. According to German dispatches, the National Socialist Party has taken down the black, red, and gold tricolor republican flag and replaced it with the old black, white, and red tricolor flag, with the National Socialist Party's swastika party emblem in the middle. However, Shanghai has not yet changed it. When asked about this matter at the German Consulate General in Shanghai yesterday, the reply was that the black, red, and gold tricolor flag is stipulated in the constitution of the Republican Germany. If the new parliament resolves to amend the article in the constitution regarding the national flag, or the president issues a special order to change the national flag, then Shanghai will immediately change it. As for the feelings of the German expatriates in this port regarding the change to the old flag, a respected person told the representative of the "North China Daily News" yesterday that the German expatriates in this port have always regretted that the black, white, and red national flag was changed to the black, red, and gold tricolor flag. However, as law-abiding citizens, they had to comply. He also said that the Germans feel that being under the black, white, and red tricolor flag is quite meaningful, because when Germany used this flag in the past, it was a world power, so everyone respected this flag. Although it is not certain whether Germany will be able to become a great power in the future, restoring the flag of the glorious era is what the Germans in Shanghai welcome.

News from the Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association After the Opening of the Membership Recruitment

The Second Shanghai Citizens' National Goods Promotion Association Membership Recruitment Conference has already opened, and the captains are enthusiastically recruiting members. Recruitment Methods

The association's members are divided into two types: national goods industrial and commercial factories and individuals. All factories that manufacture national goods, commercial firms that fully operate national goods, and male and female citizens who are enthusiastic about promoting national goods, who are over 16 years old and agree with the purpose, can fill out a volunteer form and join as members. Each captain has two types of membership volunteer forms, or you can request them by letter. In order to widely recruit individual members, the annual membership fee is one yuan.

Member Benefits

In order to encourage members to participate enthusiastically, the association stipulates that members have the right to enjoy proof of products, apply for rewards, exempt miscellaneous taxes, participate in national exhibitions, provide relief for grievances, protect interests, mediate disputes, resolve difficulties, and provide free publicity for publications, speaking, suggesting, voting, election, and being elected. In order to encourage members to use national goods, regain interests, and cultivate a spirit of saving the country, the association has reached agreements with Shanghai National Goods Company, Municipal Chamber of Commerce National Goods Market, Zhanghua Woolen Factory, National Production Tang Porcelain Sales Office, etc., to give members preferential treatment. Political Kidnapping Case Occurs on Luban Road

Korean Revolutionary Party Leader Li Chunshan Kidnapped

Our Military and Police Circles Highly Value This Matter

The mysterious and confusing kidnapping case that occurred at the entrance of Xingxing Lane, Luban Road, in the jurisdiction of the Second District General Office of the South City at 5:45 PM the day before yesterday was reported in detail in this newspaper. However, the identity of the hostage was only revealed after an investigation by the district, which found that the kidnapped person was Li Chunshan (also known as Li Yubi), the leader of the Korean Revolutionary Independence Party, who had already acquired Chinese nationality. The case is entirely politically related and cannot be compared to ordinary kidnapping for ransom. The military and police authorities in the Chinese Concession attach great importance to it and are currently doing their utmost to investigate, so that the case can be clarified as soon as possible. The details are recorded below:

Black-Plated Car Drove Away in Despair

At 5:45 PM the day before yesterday, at the entrance of Xingxing Lane, Luban Road, in the jurisdiction of the Second District General Office of the South City, passers-by were suddenly heard shouting about a kidnapping. Soon after, someone ran to the Liyuan Road Police Station, which has jurisdiction over the area, to report that a black-plated car had been parked near the entrance of Xingxing Lane. Not long after, a person riding in a rickshaw passed by, and four or five kidnappers jumped out of the car, dragged the passenger off the rickshaw, and forced him into the car. The passenger shouted that he was being kidnapped. By the time nearby residents heard the sound and rushed out, they only saw the car speeding away. Therefore, the license plate number could not be clearly identified.

Only a Fedora Hat, No Other Clues

After the incident, Jin Tian, the district chief of the district, immediately reported to the Inspectorate by telephone and tried his best to investigate. However, apart from finding a gray fedora hat belonging to the kidnapped person at the scene of the incident, there were no other clues to be found. But the result was eventually revealed: the kidnapped person was Li Chunshan, the leader of the Korean Independence Party, who had acquired Chinese nationality. Li is now 49 years old and was born in Pingshan Yijun, Korea. He is the leader of the Sino-Korean Revolutionary Alliance.

Naturalized in China, Moved to South Shanghai

On January 19th of this year, Li received Nationality Permit No. 11 issued by the Ministry of Interior of the National Government, officially changing his nationality to Chinese. His family lived at No. 54 Lubao Kangli, French Concession. However, after the January 28th Incident, Li, in view of the fact that Japanese detectives had illegally arrested Koreans in the French Concession by illegal means, and in order to protect his safety, moved to a certain place in the Chinese Concession west of the city.

Wife Jin Jingji and Children in Tow

Li's wife is named Jin Jingji, also Korean, 48 years old, and has eight children. The eldest son is only 17 years old, named Wanrong, and studies at the Sino-French School on Mintini Yin Road. The second daughter, Yingyuan, is 15 years old; the third daughter, Yingji, is 13 years old; and the fourth daughter, Yingde, is 10 years old, all studying at Lehua Girls' School. The fifth daughter, Yingqi, is 9 years old; the sixth son, Huirong, is 7 years old; and the seventh daughter, Yingba, is 5 years old, are all studying at Rencheng Elementary School. The eighth son, Junrong, is only three years old and is still in diapers.

A Sudden Change of Events on the Way to a Friend's Appointment

Because Li is Korean and a revolutionary leader, he has long been valued by imperialists, who have always wanted to get their hands on him. However, Li's whereabouts were extremely secret, and they were never successful. Li also knew that his situation was dangerous, so he usually kept a low profile and rarely went out, except when it was necessary to go out alone. He had very little contact with the outside world. Unexpectedly, at around 6 PM the day before yesterday, Li, in response to a friend's invitation, braved the rain in a rickshaw to meet Jin Zhigang, a Korean, at No. 2, Lane 190, Xingxing Lane, Luban Road, Lujiiawan, to discuss important matters. He never expected that disaster would strike as soon as he arrived at the entrance of the lane.

Three Short Bandits, Screams for Help Already Gone

As soon as Li's rickshaw arrived at the entrance of the lane, a black-plated car parked by the side of the road suddenly had three short bandits jump out. They forced Li into the car and sped away. By the time nearby residents and Li's friend, Mr. Jin, heard the screams and rushed out, the bandit's car was already gone. Only Li's fedora hat was left on the ground. They immediately ran to the Liyuan Road Police Station of the Second District General Office, which has jurisdiction over the area, and reported the matter to the General Bureau for verification.

District Chief in Difficulty Over Deadline to Solve Case

At the same time, the Municipal Authorities of the Chinese Concession, upon hearing of Mr. Li's kidnapping, paid great attention and believed that Mr. Li's kidnapping was by no means comparable to ordinary kidnapping for ransom. It must contain significant meaning. They immediately strictly ordered Jin Tian, the district chief of the Second District, which has jurisdiction over the area, to solve the case within a limited time. All Korean residents in Shanghai believed that since the January 28th Incident, the number of Korean residents in the French Concession who had moved to the Second District of the Chinese Concession was very large, and they had repeatedly requested the district government to pay attention to their protection. Now, a revolutionary leader has been kidnapped in broad daylight, and Korean residents are generally feeling insecure.

Wu Yue'e Sues Zhou Xiangyun for Abandonment

You plucked the delicate flower first,

Who would gather the withered leaves and branches?

| The complaint contains many words about the decline of beauty. |

Zhou Xiangyun, a wealthy man from Ningbo in Shanghai, is 56 years old and lives at No. 764 Niuzhuang Road. In 1915, he became acquainted with Wu Yue'e, a woman from Dongting. Recently, because Zhou abandoned Wu and ignored her, Wu hired three lawyers, Wu Kaisheng, Fan Gang, and Huang Xiubo, and filed a criminal complaint against Zhou with the First Special District Local Court for abduction and abandonment. The gist of the prosecution is as follows: the plaintiff was engaged to Mr. Lu through matchmaker Wang Zaichun in 1915, and just as they were about to set a date for the engagement ceremony, a neighbor, Mrs. Sheng (daughter of Sheng Xingsheng), told the plaintiff's mother that Zhou Xiangyun of Shanghai, who possessed great wealth, dressed in fine clothes and behaved elegantly, was young and handsome, and was seeking a divine partnership with Miss Xuanna. The plaintiff's mother politely declined, saying that Luo Fu already had a husband. However, the defendant, seeing that things were not going well, asked Mrs. Sheng to invite the plaintiff to a meeting at Yizhixiang. At the meeting, the defendant's eyes never left the plaintiff, and he was almost unable to control himself. After a whispered conversation, he proposed marriage. The plaintiff replied that she was already engaged to Mr. Lu and that it would be difficult to obtain her mother's consent. The defendant said that Mr. Lu was marrying a second wife and had three or four children from his previous wife. If she married him, she would not be free. If she married him, she would be able to do whatever she wanted and be taken care of in every way, as if she were in heaven. If she was willing to marry him, he would take care of everything. His sweet words and honeyed phrases seduced her, and she obeyed his every word. She took the opportunity to escape, and the defendant rented a room upstairs in a street-front house, which he named Long Yu (taking the meaning of clouds following the dragon), as their love nest. He invited the plaintiff to his garden, selected eight pots of peony flowers, and sent them to the residence through a gardener. He sent invitations to friends and held a grand banquet with eight tables. As a result, the news spread far and wide. The plaintiff's mother disowned the plaintiff as her daughter, and Mr. Lu, upon hearing the news, was ashamed to be associated with the plaintiff and declared that the marriage was off. The defendant, seeing that his scheme had succeeded, immediately closed the affair and moved to No. 100 Qinshouli, Jing'an Temple Road, where he lived with the defendant for two years. He paid her 200 yuan per month. The plaintiff repeatedly urged him to fulfill his promise and marry her. The defendant claimed that it was difficult because the plaintiff had not yet given birth to a child. Therefore, he had adopted a daughter in her name for the plaintiff to raise, named Chongxi. From then on, the monthly allowance was only 150 yuan. The plaintiff often complained about the delay in marriage and the reduction in expenses. The defendant came only once or twice a week, and the monthly allowance was often less than 150 yuan. The plaintiff had to raise the girl, which was very expensive, but the monthly allowance was reduced, making it impossible to maintain. Every time they met, there was an argument. Therefore, since 1929, he had disappeared and had not paid any expenses. When she sent someone to invite him, it was like throwing stones into the sea. When they met by chance, he treated her like a stranger. Helplessly, she took the girl to the defendant's mansion, but the gate was heavily guarded, and she had to return empty-handed many times. However, the mother and daughter were alone, living in poverty for five or six years, pawning and borrowing everything they could, and were about to be overwhelmed by debt. The future was bleak and unbearable. The plaintiff believes that her youth, personality, and reputation have been ruined by the defendant. Now she is almost forty years old, her face is fading, and it is difficult to find another marriage partner. As the saying goes, "You plucked the delicate flower first, who would gather the withered leaves and branches?" Her heart is filled with sorrow, and tears wet her clothes. Over time, she has developed an illness. Although she is still alive, her anger is difficult to quell. In addition to filing a separate civil suit for the debts owed and alimony, she has compiled the above facts and requested your court to summon the defendant Zhou Xiangyun to court and punish him according to Article 315 of the Criminal Law and Paragraph 1 of Article 309 of the same law. Yesterday morning, at 10:30, Judge Feng Shide of the Criminal Court of the First Special Court opened the first criminal court to summon Zhou Xiangyun, who arrived with his agents, the three lawyers He, Li, and Peng. First, Wu Yue'e testified that she was 42 years old, from Dongting Mountain, and currently lived at No. 20, Lane 60, Weihaiwei Road. In 1915, the defendant, because he wanted to marry her but failed, designed to have her hang up a sign as a prostitute, so that the Lu family would withdraw from the marriage. His plan succeeded, and he rented a house with her in Qinshoufang. When she hung up the sign as a prostitute, only the defendant accompanied her in and out, as everyone knew. At first, the defendant paid her monthly expenses, but since 1929, he had stopped paying, so she had no choice but to sue. When Zhou Xiangyun was questioned, he claimed that he had never met the plaintiff before and that they had never met. The claim of cohabitation was even more unfounded. Zhou's lawyer then stated that there was a procedural issue in this case that should be investigated and ruled on first. The abandonment alleged by the plaintiff occurred in 1929, and according to the law, the sentence was also less than one year. Therefore, even if the defendant had committed this act, it would be covered by the amnesty. According to Article 310 of the Criminal Law, he should be exempt from prosecution. Furthermore, even if the abduction was only discovered in 1929, according to the law, the statute of limitations for prosecution is six months. Now that the plaintiff has filed a lawsuit after the statute of limitations has expired, the case should be ruled inadmissible. He requested the court to rule on the above two points first. Judge Feng then ordered that the matter be reviewed and handled. The plaintiff's lawyer, Fan Gang, immediately stated that the defendant in this case was trying to deny everything in court today, even claiming that he had never met the plaintiff. He requested that the defendant be ordered to provide bail within a revised timeframe. Judge Feng granted the request and ordered Zhou to submit a bail bond to the court within three days.

Ming Garden Lawsuit Dismissed

| Martin Not Liable for Compensation |

The lawsuit filed by the Dog Racing Association against Martin, the current Assistant Inspector-General of the Public Works Department, and former Chairman of the Board of Directors, Mcnaghten, for damages of $2,500,001 due to the closure of the Ming Garden Dog Racing Track by the Public Works Department, was dismissed in relation to Mcnaghten after a ruling by British Judge Grier. Now, the part of the lawsuit against Martin was also decided by the jury the day before yesterday, stating that there were no damages that could be compensated. It was declared that the activities of the Dog Racing Association in Ming Garden were sufficient to hinder order and good government in the concession and were a public nuisance. Martin believed that his actions were under the command of the Public Works Department in the implementation of the Yangjingbang Regulations and were justified. The Public Works Department also had the right to issue the closure order. Judge Grier then formally ruled to dismiss the lawsuit based on the jury's decision, with court costs borne by the plaintiff. This case of the Dog Racing Association has been involved in litigation repeatedly. After the first ruling by the British Consular Court was dismissed, an appeal was filed. Last year, the appellate court overturned the original verdict and ordered a retrial. Now, it has been retried and ruled by Judge Grier.

Reactions to the Collection of Sampan Boat Donations in Wusong

Rowing Sampans to Make a Living

Going to the Party Headquarters to Request a Reduction by Half

The Wusong Boat Donation Office of the Shanghai Municipal Finance and Public Utilities Bureau has recently sent personnel to collect registration fees of three yuan for sampan ferries in Cao Bang, as well as monthly donations of six cents per month starting from January 1933, totaling one yuan and eight cents for three months, amounting to four yuan and eight cents. Those sampans that were unable to pay had their oars and oils confiscated, causing their business to be suspended and their livelihoods to be cut off. Forced by desperation, dozens of sampan men, women, old and young gathered and went to the Eighth District Party Headquarters to petition, and submitted a request to the directors of the Municipal Finance and Public Utilities Bureau, requesting a reduction in the levy to maintain their livelihoods. The reasons given were that Wusong's situation was different from Shanghai's, and the prosperity and decline of their businesses were very different. Moreover, they suffered greatly during last year's war, which greatly damaged their vitality. After the war, business declined, and their livelihoods were not enough to make ends meet. Housing in the town was scarce, and rents had increased several times, making it impossible for them to rent a place to live. Most of them lived on their boats and made a living by rowing passengers. They only earned two or three copper coins for each passenger. They endured all kinds of hardships every day, such as bitter cold, wind, frost, rain, and scorching heat. Their miserable situation was probably the worst in the world. Moreover, they often encountered strong winds and rainstorms on the way, when the stars and moon were not visible, making it extremely dangerous. The hardship was beyond description. Wang Chengye, a standing committee member of the Eighth District Party Headquarters, agreed to consult with the Boat Donation Office and handle the matter. The men and women were satisfied and dispersed after being told to wait for a solution.

Frequent Spring Snowfall, Chilly Spring Weather, Difficult to Quickly Disperse the Poor from the Shelter

Temporarily Continue to Provide Care

The Shanghai Charitable Organizations Joint Association's Temporary Shelter in South Shanghai is still providing care for more than 1,000 poor people. It was originally scheduled to close at the end of March, but due to the frequent spring snow and the extremely cold weather, the poor people, hearing that they would be dispersed, felt that they would still have no way to make a living after leaving the shelter, and all cried bitterly. The administrator of the shelter, Mr. Zhang Zixin, in order to save people thoroughly, plans to temporarily continue to provide care for the poor people in the shelter and disperse them only when the weather is warmer. He is not too concerned about the expenses and is trying to save on all items. However, the cost of rice for the poor people is still high. The two philanthropists, Wang Yiting and Huang Hanzhi, members of the association, had previously written to all sectors of society to encourage donations. It has been heard that the donors include China General Edison Company with 500 yuan, Zhang Yuqingtang with 150 yuan, Huang Hanzhi with 100 yuan, and Huaiyu with 30 yuan. It is hoped that all philanthropists will continue to donate so that the shelter can continue to operate.

Yeyuan Amusement Fair Opens Today

The Jiangwan Yeyuan, initiated by Shanghai philanthropist Wang Yiting and others, is using the beautiful weather and scenery to launch a charity amusement fair. It has been decided that starting today (11th), it will begin to welcome entries for various innovative and elegant amusement items. The categories have been previously published in this newspaper. It is heard that the entry time is from 1:30 PM to 5:00 PM every day, and will be postponed in case of rain. It is also heard that from this day on, China General Omnibus will have many vehicles running directly to the front of the park.

Garment Industry Association Raises Donations for Aviation to Save the Country

Shanghai Garment Industry Association Standing Committee Members Wu Zhihao, Cui Jiefu, Lu Qisheng, Hao Haishan, Xi Xiaoyun, etc., in view of the fact that our army's resistance against the enemy often suffers from enemy aircraft attacks if there is no aircraft assistance, Shanghai's various groups have raised donations for aviation to save the country, and the garment industry is also unwilling to fall behind. They held a banquet at Hongyunlou last night, with dozens of people including Chuan Tingfang, Zhang Zikang, and Tang Puming. The chairman Wu Zhihao first stated the reasons for the meeting, saying that now that the country is in trouble, and in addition to the heavy rain today, everyone has worked hard and actively participated, which shows that the people's hearts have not died and that there is still hope for the country. Our army lacks aircraft and air defense equipment to resist the enemy, and it is especially important to purchase them as soon as possible. It is hoped that all those present will donate generously and work together to overcome the national crisis, so that our army and national defense will both benefit. More than 4,000 yuan was raised on the spot, and the list is listed below: Wu Zhihao, Lu Qisheng, Futai, Jinchang, Xingji, Gongyi, Yuxiang Gong, the above seven households each donated 200 yuan. Baocheng, Baotai, Yulong, Detai, Taifeng, Yuanyu, Yuankang, Xiangfeng, Tiantian, Shengji, Hefeng, Puji, Cuifeng, Xinyuan, Yongyuan, Jintai, Deyuan, Zhang Zikang, the above eighteen households each donated 100 yuan. Qiaoyuan, Gantai, Tongtai, Shen Xiehe, Xiepin, Tongtai, Tongfeng, Yuanfeng, Yuanchang, Zhang Fengyuan, Hao Haishan, Ye Xingfang, Zhou Zuoqing, Tang Jinming, the above fourteen households each donated 50 yuan. You Jichen, He Shuxiang, Dingji, the above three households each donated 30 yuan. The rest are still being solicited, and the total will be considerable.

National Medical Center's Shanghai Branch Hosts the Press

Reports on the Future Direction of the Center

The Organization Method is Divided into Four Steps

Chinese medicine has a history of more than 4,000 years, with inventions in every generation. However, due to the lack of a unified advocacy organization, and with family learning and apprenticeship, it is inevitably complicated. Therefore, Mr. Tan Yankai, Chen Guofu, Chen Lifu, Jiao Yitang, and other gentlemen suggested to the Central Political Conference that a National Medical Center be established, using scientific methods to organize, improve the treatment of diseases, and methods of making medicine. This was decided in seventy-six National Affairs Conferences, and the Executive Yuan was instructed to prepare for the establishment of the Central National Medical Center and ordered all provinces and cities to establish branches to promote it. The Shanghai branch was established on January 15th of this year. In order to actively organize Chinese medicine and publicize the efficacy of Chinese medicine, the center hosted the press at Yizhixiang last night. More than 80 people, including reporters from various newspapers, famous doctors, and Lu Zhong'an, director of the center, attended. During the meeting, Chairman Cai Jiben reported on the center's future work direction, saying that the current method of organizing Chinese medicine has been divided into four steps: (1) First, investigate the medical situation of the city

Another Dog Case

Dispute Over a Sick Dog

The lawsuit of the Ming Garden Dog Racing Track was just concluded the day before yesterday, but yesterday the British Consular Court had another lawsuit regarding damages related to dog racing, as if it were an aftershock. This time, a valuable race dog named John Haig suffered from arthritis in one toe of its left front leg. The plaintiff, Fudge, accused the defendant, Guo Date, of negligence of duty, resulting in the injury, and demanded compensation for damages. The defendant denied negligence of duty and responsibility for the dog's injury. The case is currently being tried by a Justice Shi of the court.

Situation and prepare statistics for organization. When performing duties, local authorities must be asked for assistance when necessary; (2) Establish an Academic Research Committee, with seventeen to twenty-nine members, and organize them into departments; (3) Establish an Academic Guidance Committee. To promote open academic research, eminent Chinese and Western medical experts will be invited to be members; (4) Allocate regular expenses. The board of directors has decided that for every prescription written by a doctor in the city, a center fee of one cent will be attached. Each doctor will first send the prescription to the center to pay the fee and stamp it, and a receipt will be issued at any time. Pharmacies will recognize this stamp as proof of a legitimate doctor and sell medicine accordingly. Prescriptions for diagnosis and treatment in Shantang Hospital and prescriptions for self-medication by patients may be exempted as appropriate. The organization of the center, in addition to establishing various academic research committees, has two vice-directors and thirty-seven directors. All matters related to the organization of Chinese medical academics and business, the improvement of Chinese medicine, and the management, supervision, and other matters are within the scope of the center's responsibility.

Opening and Dredging of the Puhui Pond Determined

Municipal Councilors Request Additional Budget

The opening and dredging of the Puhui Pond in West Shanghai was initiated by Ma Xiangbo, an elderly man of ninety-four years. It was later diverted and dredged to Songjiang and Qingpu counties, and construction has begun. It is learned that the Shanghai section has been divided into six sections by the Public Works Bureau for bidding. Yesterday afternoon at 2:00, the bids were opened publicly in the Public Works Bureau. Huang Rixin, the audit director of the Third Section of the Municipal Government, was sent by the Municipal Government to supervise, and Wu Hengzhong, secretary of the Disaster Relief Committee of the National Government, and Municipal Councilors also attended the ceremony. As a result of the bidding, Shen Rongji won the first, fourth, and fifth sections, Lu Yuelou won the second section, Zhang Zhensheng won the third section, and Wang Lianji won the sixth section, with a total bid price of 111,006 yuan, 5 jiao, 6 fen, and 8 li. However, the city's budget is only 100,000 yuan. According to the budget, the amount of earthwork must be reduced. Yang Xinzheng, Chen Yaofu, and others have requested Director Shen to submit the request to the Municipal Government to add to the budget, because the councilors have a close relationship with the river, which has been blocked for a long time. According to the bureau's calculations, the amount of earthwork cannot be reduced any further. Director Shen has agreed to submit the request.

Enthusiastic Relief for Disaster Areas in Northeast China

Qu Yingguang Replies and Agrees to Go North The Shanghai Charitable Organizations Joint Association's Northeast Refugee Relief Joint Association sent Qu Wenliu as a representative to the Northeast for investigation. After returning to Shanghai, he returned to his hometown of Ninghai for official duties. The association has repeatedly telegraphed him to come to Shanghai and go to Pingjin to preside over everything. The association received a reply from Mr. Qu yesterday, saying, "Dear Sir, I have received your telegram. Since you have not abandoned me and have an agreement with Mr. Yang, I will obey your orders and go north. I will leave for Shanghai on the 10th to receive your instructions. Please raise funds for relief so that I can take them with me for relief. We will meet soon. I will not go into details. I wish you well."

Philippine Overseas Chinese Remit Donations The association also received a letter from the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce in Legazpi, Philippines, yesterday, saying, "Dear Sir, since the eastern neighbor invaded, it has been more than a year, and our compatriots have been groaning under the iron hooves of the tyrannical Japanese every moment. We, as nationals, although far away overseas, if we are not made of wood or stone, how can we not be moved? The Chinese Consul General in the Philippines (Xu Kun) has allocated two donation books to your association. We have raised 163 Philippine pesos, which were remitted to your association by the Consul General stationed in Manila on the 24th of this month. We hope you will take note and remit the funds to the disaster areas in Northeast China to help the refugees, doing our duty as citizens."

Jiangbei Man and Woman Cleverly Abduct Songjiang Girl

Passengers Had Different Tickets

Accents and Circumstances Differed

At the Fanwangdu Station on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway, at around 5 PM yesterday, when the No. 39 slow train, which had departed from the Zhakou at 10 AM, arrived, three passengers, an old woman, a man, and a girl, disembarked at Fanwangdu. The old woman and the man spoke with a Jiangbei accent, but the girl spoke with a Songjiang accent. The railway police officer at the station, Bo Yunlong, found the trio suspicious, questioned them, and their answers were evasive. Upon checking the man and woman's tickets, they had boarded at Songjiang and purchased tickets to Fanwangdu Station. However, the girl's half-price ticket was from Songjiang to the North Station. It was clear that there was an abduction involved, so the man, woman, and girl were all detained and taken to the railway police chief at the South Station for questioning. The police chief, Wang Youzhang, first questioned the man, who identified himself as Wang Lianyou, 34 years old, from Yancheng. He stated, "I met the old woman, Shan Changshi, at Miss Lu Da's house. Today, I traveled with her from Songjiang to Fanwangdu Station to visit my elder sister. I don't know the girl who is with the old woman; she was brought by the old woman. I helped the old woman take a rickshaw after getting off at Fanwangdu Station, and out of kindness, I asked the girl to ride in the rickshaw with me. I intended to send her to my relatives, not to abduct her." The old woman stated her name was Shan Changshi, 60 years old, from Yancheng. She said, "I don't know the man who came with me; I only met him at Songjiang Station while waiting for the train. I also don't know the girl. When boarding the train at the station, he asked me to come to Shanghai with him, and I agreed. He bought his own ticket. At Fanwangdu Station, the girl got off the train with me. When the man hired a rickshaw for me, the police came to question us, and we were detained." The girl stated her name was Zhang A'nan, 10 years old, from Songjiang. Her father's name is Zhang Changyu, and they live near Songjiang Station. "Today, I was playing at the station when I met an old woman and a man, both of whom I didn't know. They both said they would take me to Shanghai to find my mother and that Shanghai would be a fun place to play. The old woman gave me a ticket, and I boarded the train with them. The three of us sat together on the train. After getting off, the old woman asked me to ride in a rickshaw with her to go to Fanwangdu to find my mother. Just as we were about to get on the rickshaw and leave, the police brought us here, and we couldn't leave." After questioning by Police Chief Wang, the statements were found to be inconsistent, clearly indicating a joint abduction, which could not be denied. Furthermore, the tickets purchased by the suspect Wang Lianyou and the woman Shan Changshi were from Songjiang Station to Fanwangdu Station, but the half-price ticket purchased for the girl Zhang A'nan was from Songjiang to the North Station. This was undoubtedly a calculated plan to have the girl sit in the same car and avoid suspicion during questioning. Given that this case involved abduction, separating family members, and was indeed unlawful, a written report was prepared, and police were dispatched to escort them to the local court for questioning.

Zheng Buxiang's Cause of Death Unknown

Male Corpse Beside the Beijing-Shanghai Railway

At around 2 AM yesterday, police officers Tian Xiancheng and Liu Junde from the Tanzhiwan Sub-Bureau of the Zhabei Fourth District Public Security Bureau were patrolling near the Beijing-Shanghai Railway (behind Yangongtang), about three li west of the Dayang Bridge. They noticed an umbrella and used a flashlight to investigate further. They then discovered a male corpse lying beside the tracks. Initially suspecting that he had been hit by a train, they immediately returned to the station to report the incident. Inspector Ge Weirui immediately dispatched Police Chief Wang Junjie, along with police officers, and summoned the local headman Zhang Fengqi to investigate. They found a gunshot wound near the left ear of the deceased, with the bullet still lodged inside. They also found two six-inch White Langlin pistol shell casings near the body, along with the umbrella, and took them all to the station. They also instructed the headman to report the incident to the Shanghai Local Court for an autopsy. The court then appointed a prosecutor and a coroner to examine the body in the afternoon and instructed the family to claim the body and await the arrest of the murderer for interrogation. It was later learned that the deceased was Zheng Buxiang, 25 years old, from Yancheng. His elderly mother, Zheng Zhengshi, lives at No. 289, East Panjiaqiao, in the Dafeng Yarn Factory workers' quarters. He had previously served as a patrol officer in the concession for a long time. Perhaps he was assassinated by a criminal gang because of this.

Two Fires

At around 5 AM yesterday, a fire broke out in a straw shed in the Baojiazhai area of Huayuan Road in the Nanshi district. The flames quickly spread, engulfing the roof. In an instant, nine straw sheds were destroyed. Fire brigades from various districts rushed to the scene to extinguish the fire. It took over half an hour to put it out. The arsonist, Ding Shaozhang, was detained by the local Public Security Bureau for investigation.

At 1:30 PM yesterday, a fire broke out at the home of Zhang Yunhong at No. 80 Haichang Road, Zhabei, due to carelessness while cooking, leaving a fire unattended outside the stove. The fire quickly spread, affecting the neighboring houses at Nos. 82 and 83, resulting in the destruction of three houses in total. The Zhabei Second Section Fire Brigade arrived and extinguished the fire after some time.

Inauguration of the 24th Branch of the Municipal Federation

The 24th District Branch (Beijing Road) of the Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Federation held an inauguration ceremony yesterday. Chairman Wang Xiaolai held the swearing-in ceremony and then elected officers. Wang Xiaolai, Shen Tianxin, Zhang Yizhai, Yi Zhetang, and Yu Zhongxian were elected as standing committee members, Yang Guangxing and Hu Hongbin as general affairs officers, Zhou Qishi, Zhou Hongquan, Chen Yongzhong, and Chen Shengfu as mediators, and Zhou Zhixing, Wang Shaofu, and Qi Wancai as publicity officers. Zhang Shuliang and Ni Genghua were elected as organizing officers. Following this, discussions were held. (1) Regarding the letter from the Municipal Federation concerning the organization of a National Goods Movement branch, it was resolved that (A) all executive committee members of this branch would be ex-officio members and (B) the standing committee would convene a meeting of enthusiastic members of the National Goods Movement to establish the branch as soon as possible. (2) Regarding the letter from Executive Committee member Zhang Shuliang requesting to resign due to being overburdened with affairs, it was resolved to persuade him to stay. The rest is omitted.

Chinese Electric Company Union

Negotiating Pension Issues

Since 1925, the Chinese Electric Company, out of consideration for the hardship of its workers, on the proposal of the company's deputy manager, Zhu Kongjia, allocated a portion of the company's annual public dividends as a pension fund for aging workers, that is, a public reserve fund. To date, it has accumulated 94,000 yuan. Currently, due to unequal treatment by the company, these funds have been allocated to employees, which the entire workforce strongly opposes. They are demanding that the company allocate all funds to the workers for equal distribution. Upon hearing this, the First District Water and Electricity Industry Union, fearing a labor strike, dispatched executive director Tan Honglin and others to mediate and guide the entire workforce. The union is actively engaging with the company to negotiate and has submitted a request to the party and government authorities for a fair resolution, awaiting mediation.

Publishing World

[Dongbei Zhanshi] (Northeast Warriors) by Zhang Jianxin, which has been published before, [Shi Jiu Lu Jun Ge Da Xue Xuesheng Yiyong Jun] (The 19th Route Army and University Student Volunteers) by Zhang Jianxin, a student of the training class, went to the Northeast to participate in volunteer army work after the end of the Shanghai war. Now, Mr. Zhang has written a lengthy war novel [Dongbei Zhanshi] (Northeast Warriors) in his spare time from military affairs, which is about 100,000 words long and published by Xing Shi Wenyi Publishing House, and is sold by Shanghai Xiandai Bookstore. All bookstores in the country have agents for the book. Since the book was published, all libraries, schools, and patriotic people have purchased and read it enthusiastically. Some junior high schools have also designated it as a supplementary reading material for students.

Shanghai Municipal Council Legal Department Work Report for the Previous Year

Barrister Boland, Head of the Legal Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council, stated in his 1932 report that a total of 101,517 cases were prosecuted in the Shanghai First Special District Local Court and the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. Among them, 74,698 cases were minor bylaw cases, and the defendants did not appear in court, and the bail was confiscated to close the case. There were also 602 cases that were withdrawn due to insufficient evidence. Excluding the above two items, there were 26,217 criminal cases prosecuted and completed, of which 24,222 were found guilty after trial, and 1,975 were acquitted. The proportion of sentences imposed on the number of prosecutions was 92.2%. In addition, there were 1,078 criminal private prosecution cases and 3,181 cases of violations of health and public works regulations prosecuted by the two courts, and 5,591 cases of violations of traffic regulations prosecuted by the Traffic Department of the Police Department.

Public and Private Appeals Cases

The Municipal Council filed a total of 55 appeals, including those not concluded from the previous year. 44 cases were concluded, with the result that 48 cases were dismissed, 3 cases were withdrawn, 19 cases were given heavier sentences, and 4 cases were remanded for retrial. As for the cases appealed by the defendants, including those not concluded from the previous year, a total of 66 cases, 497 cases have been concluded, as follows: 314 appeals dismissed, 27 appeals withdrawn, 30 acquittals, 89 sentences reduced, 7 sentences increased, 19 cases remanded for retrial, 1 released for medical treatment, and 2 exempted from prosecution due to amnesty.

Situation of Transfer Proposals

In this year, official authorities outside the concession requested a total of 172 cases, involving 359 people. Among them, the evidence against 308 people was sufficient, and they have been transferred. Another 9 people were released at the request of the Legal Department due to insufficient evidence. 12 people were released on bail pending trial, and 5 people were released on bail ordering them to surrender themselves to the competent authorities. 2 people were immediately tried and punished by the concession court because they were found to have committed crimes in the concession. Another 2 people were transferred at the request of the Hong Kong police, and the concession court decided to try them itself. Another person was withdrawn from prosecution by the original requesting authority. In addition, 2 criminals released under amnesty were transferred at the request of the authorities because they had committed crimes outside the concession. There was also a German who was extradited at the request of his consul.

Unresolved Cases and Probation

As of December 31, 1932, there were a total of 52 unresolved cases in the High Court and the Local Court, and 130 unresolved cases of speed trials and appeals, for a total of 182 unresolved cases. There were 556 cases of probation this year, and 17 cases of probation due to appeal.

Stamp Duty and Cigarette Cases

There were 119 cases of violations of the stamp tax regulations, with penalties ranging from ten yuan to four hundred eighty yuan. There were 55 cigarette tax cases prosecuted, and 53 cases have been fined. There were also three cases of trademark infringement and one case of property infringement, which were handled by the Cigarette Special Patrol Team for factual convenience. The Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance expressed great satisfaction with the work of the team.

Letter

To the Editor, We have recently read in the news column of your newspaper on the 10th that the Yu (presumably a mistake for Yu) Jiang Steamer, which had been missing for a long time, had sunk off Hainan Island, and claimed that it was overladen with coal and suffered misfortune in the face of a hurricane, etc. The fact that the Yu Long Steamer sailed from Hongji on December 8th of last year and went missing in March is indeed true. However, although our company has tried its best to inquire with all parties concerned, there is still no evidence to support the news that the ship has sunk. However, in order to understand the whereabouts of the ship, we are still continuing to investigate in all directions. Furthermore, according to the Yu Long Steamer, the weight of the ship is 2,700 tons, and the coal loaded this time is less than 2,450 tons, there is no overloading situation, all of which are corrected to correct the truth and avoid the public from hearing. This is to request the Master of the Shen Bao to understand. Yu Long Steamer Co., Ltd. March 10th.

To the Editor, We recently read the news in the third page of your newspaper that the anti-Japanese paintings in the cigarettes of the Shanghai Fuxin Tobacco Company are enemy goods. We were shocked to hear this. The anti-Japanese paintings used by the Fuxin Company are all printed by our company. The paper materials used by our company are all purchased from various paper shops and have invoices and vouchers to prove, and are by no means enemy goods. Our company has always been patriotic, and how could we use enemy goods? Now the Fuxin Company has seriously negotiated with several companies. This matter concerns the reputation of the company. In addition to sending a letter to the guild requesting correction, our company shall be responsible for all adverse results caused by the enemy goods. I hereby write to your newspaper, and I request you to correct it. To the Shen Bao. Fuhua Printing Company. March 10th.

Weather Report

Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 pm yesterday: The Shandong coast and the Yellow Sea are cold and cloudy, with strong northwest to north winds and local snowfall. The Yangtze River Basin and the coast here are cold and cloudy, gradually clearing, with heavy fog or rain, strong winds from the north to northeast. The coastal area south of Ma'anshan Island is cloudy, with rain and strong northeast winds. Southern Japan has tight cyclone rain. Also, before 3:00 pm yesterday, the temperature in this city within 24 hours was 40.2 at the highest and 34.5 at the lowest. On the same day last year, the highest was 58.6 and the lowest was 46.6.

Reader Consultant

Women's Liberation and Family Problems

丨Letter from Ms. Yang Yuwen of Hankou丨

I have a difficult problem and ask you to sacrifice a little of your precious time to give me concrete guidance. Unfortunately, I lost my mother early and have suffered all the hardships of the world. Fortunately, I studied for several years and gained some knowledge. Unexpectedly, my stubborn father, when I was only one year away from graduating high school, used coercive means to marry me off to a completely unfamiliar and extremely corrupt family. At that time, because I had been studying at school for a long time, I did not understand the situation of old families at all. I thought that with a dowry of one thousand yuan, I could continue my studies after marriage. But I didn’t know that my mother-in-law's family not only refused but also said some sarcastic remarks. Less than a year later, I gave birth to a daughter. So, the matter of studying was temporarily put aside. I am focusing on raising my child so that she becomes a useful person and serves the country. This is my obligation to the country. However, the environment does not allow me to do this. If I compromise to the environment, my mental and physical suffering will be too great, and I will definitely have difficulty living out my natural lifespan. Since coming to my mother-in-law's house, in less than half a year, I have contracted asthma and nearly died! My death is not a big deal, but I do not want my child to suffer the pain of losing a mother again. Alas, sir, you must not understand the plight of being a daughter-in-law in an old-fashioned family. My blunt pen cannot describe even one ten-thousandth of it. In short, my mother-in-law is extremely cunning, vicious, and fierce. Her poor mouth is always on me all day long, and I really have no peace of mind or sleep. Sometimes she even listens to the instigation of my younger sister-in-law, younger uncle, and servants and scolds me severely and threatens to hit me, making me helpless. I have no choice but to kneel down and apologize to make her stop. No matter how they abuse me, I am not allowed to utter a sound or shed a tear, because my mother-in-law says that if there is any slight displeasure in her family, she will not spare us. Sir! People are not made of wood or stone, how can they not be worried and get sick! Every time I want to get out of this dark family, but there is no ill will between my husband and me, and I especially can't bear to leave my little darling! My child is almost half a year old, so I have to swallow my anger and barely survive. Ah, for all eternity, when will I be able to escape this hell on earth! To say something against my conscience, my mother-in-law is young. Even if I wait until my hair turns white, it will be difficult to have my voice heard. As for separation, it is impossible, because her family has always advocated a large family system. Not only will it not succeed, but she will also say that I am alienating her mother-son relationship, and the family finances cannot be divided. Especially my husband, who is only nineteen years old (more than five years younger than me) and has never been to school (his Chinese is very good), has not lost his boyishness and is very afraid of his mother. How can he save me from the sea of suffering! There are many brothers, and exclusively dividing up a little ancestral property is ultimately not a good plan. My temperament has always been upright, and I am unwilling to live a life worse than that of an inhuman. Thinking about the fundamental reason why women are persecuted, it is nothing more than the fact that they cannot be economically independent. I urgently need a job now, but I have no special skills. Where can I find a job? I am thinking of going to a cram school while also taking time to go to a certain school to learn sewing and weaving, but who will take care of my nursing infant? How can I get the permission of those stubborn people? If this last glimmer of hope fails, if I am bullied by them again, I will definitely implement a separation or divorce. Please tell me the procedures for separation or divorce. Will my maternal family interfere? As a weak and helpless woman with no one to rely on, being within the sphere of influence of the evil forces of my maternal and marital families, can I prevail in law? And can my beloved child be raised by me to adulthood? This is the biggest problem! Kind-hearted sir who helps the world, please guide this lost lamb!

Answer: Reply to the letter briefly as follows: (1) The lady's family pain is a general phenomenon of old Chinese families. For the present, the best way is to resolutely abandon everything and go out to seek independent living. This method is the most thorough and straightforward. Considering the lady's intentions, I am afraid that this level cannot be achieved, so one must (2) discuss with your husband and the two of you think of a way to make a living. Or ask your husband to come out to make a living first, or you come out to make a living first. I think your writing is very fluent and your handwriting is also very neat. If you can find a clerical job, there will be a way, because the reason why you are suffering from family pain is because you cannot be economically independent. Economic independence will solve more than half of the problem. However, since your husband is a "boyish" nineteen-year-old youth and does not have the courage to resist the old family, then I can't think of a perfect solution. (3) There is another way: first, encourage your father-in-law to come out to study and let him come to a big city to breathe the civilization of the industrial society. Perhaps it will slowly digest his boyishness. However, there is also a danger here that the lady must consider. That is, if he really absorbs the civilized air of industry and builds up his courage to resist the old family, then his vision will inevitably increase. Since you are a few years older than him, are you afraid that he will "see something different and move his heart" and "abandon the old and seek the new"? But for the time being, you don't have to worry too much. If he really treats you unfairly at that time, you can step aside or take your child and live your own life, and you will have nothing to be ashamed of. At present, if a woman is determined to get rid of a evil family, the law will not have any forced obedience.
