Free Talk

On the Subject of Slaves of a Conquered Nation

— Wang Renshu

With the loss of Rehe, the gentry and the like are said to be preparing to become slaves of a conquered nation. I think this is somewhat Quixotic.

Before Don Quixote's great battle with the windmill, he had treated the inn as a royal city, and the innkeeper as an emperor, and had been knighted. Now, there is actually a group of gentry who want to treat this autumn-leaf-like territory as their own country, and receive the [slave of a conquered nation] knighting by the Japanese clogs. That is truly a unique Don Quixote.

When the January 28th Incident broke out last year, I once heard a high-ranking military officer in Hankou say: Our current major problem is not the Japanese. We would rather let the Japanese occupy Hankou than let the XX army occupy it. In my opinion, this is indeed the truth. Of course, that high-ranking military officer has his own position. To put it bluntly, if Hankou is occupied by the Japanese, he can still be his military officer; isn't Zhang Haipeng a precedent? However, if XX army occupies it, what will happen? Obviously, he is in danger of having his head moved. His class consciousness is very correct.

But from another perspective, China no longer has something like a country, or at least China has to be put in parentheses. But since the Opium War, imperialism has already partially taken China as its own colony. The three northeastern provinces were not lost since the September 18th Incident, but had already been lost before the September 18th Incident. The demise of China will not start from today, but has already been lost to the hands of various imperialists. All rulers become rulers only after being knighted by various imperialists. Who can explain that the Battle of Rehe is a sign that our people are unwilling to be slaves of a conquered nation? Who can point out that this is not a civil war between various knighted Don Quixotes? Then, because of the loss of Rehe, the gentry and the like want to receive the knighting of a slave of a conquered nation, which is really a step behind. And in fact, the gentry and the like who have already worn [an old, rusty helmet passed down from their great-grandfather and left in the corner of the house for a long time] have no need to ask the clogs for a second knighting.

For the present plan, it is better for the gentry to still follow those figures like Tang Yulin and move to Rehe, or even Liaoning, to live. As for the adults and gentlemen who have high opinions and want to clean their houses, so that [small mice] do not jump on the beams, and welcome the dwarves, blue-eyed people, and straight-footed ghosts to have a [carving party] to their heart's content, that is just blindly learning the tricks of Don Quixote, treating windmills as giants; and the result is: [He shielded himself, carried a spear and horse, and chased the first windmill, stabbing the spear into the car shed. The windmill rolled the spear away with violent force. In an instant, the shaft of the spear was shattered. The knight and horse were thrown into the wilderness with the spear, turning around and falling to the ground.]

That's all. Then, at that time, it would be more appropriate for the gentry and the like to move back home and receive the knighting of a slave of a conquered nation from the windmills again.

Lamenting Tang Yulin

— Yang Qiu

Rehe was finally [lost] again. According to a certain important person: [The loss of Rehe was expected,] 丨丨Naturally, everyone knows that this was [expected,] but now this [expected] has made our Chairman Tang Yulin a target of public criticism, and he has also been [removed from office and investigated] by a clear order.

If Tang Yulin's removal from office and investigation was before Rehe was [lost], and the reason for the removal from office and investigation was because he imposed exorbitant taxes in Rehe, because he forced the planting of opium in Rehe, because he manufactured and sold red pills, morphine, and heroin in Rehe, because he squeezed the bone marrow and devoured the blood in Rehe, harming the people to indulge in himself, we would inevitably applaud and applaud. However, this fact happened after Rehe was [lost], and the reason was not for the above-mentioned reasons, but because of the [expected] loss of Rehe, then, Tang Yulin's dismissal and investigation is unjust, and the matter is lamentable!

Why do we say that Tang Yulin's removal from office and investigation is [unjust]? Is the dismissal and investigation not because of his [non-resistance]? Is it not because of his [abandoning the city and fleeing]? But who should be responsible for the fall of the three northeastern provinces? Who should be responsible for the fall of Jinzhou and Yuguan? Our young marshal is still holding a large army and living in Beiping, dancing, listening to Peking opera, and playing golf, isn't he? Why should our Chairman Tang be dismissed and investigated?

However, to put it another way, our Chairman Tang is indeed [guilty]. His crime is not in [non-resistance] and [abandoning the city and fleeing], but in not being good at using [resistance strategies]. The facts of the past two years have not taught our Chairman Tang to be smart. In this regard, Tang Yulin is too stupid to live.

We plan for Chairman Tang. His final [resistance plan] should be like this:

First stage: (The Japanese army has the appearance of invading Rehe) Send a telegram to the whole country, expressing [determination to resist]: issue a statement, expressing [oath to defend the land to the death], be generous and passionate, so that the [people] of the whole country absolutely believe.

Second stage: (The Japanese army actually launches an attack) While negotiating, resist, that is, submit a [serious protest] to Japan, using hard words such as [all responsibility should be borne by the Japanese side] to [scare] the Japanese army. If the Japanese army is hard [scared] and does not retreat, then on the other hand, you have to put down the opium pipe, set up a battle, and show [resistance], even if a few people are sacrificed as a result, but in any case, it will never sacrifice your own name.

Third stage: (The Japanese army is getting closer and closer) In diplomacy, appeal to the League of Nations and Washington, requesting to uphold justice: in strategy, establish a new position, [lure the enemy deep], to annihilate them in one fell swoop; in propaganda, send a telegram to the whole country, reporting that our army has captured and killed a number of enemy rebels, and report what is lacking in the front, calling on the [people] to go to the national crisis together and donate generously.

Fourth stage: (Of course, the Japanese army is approaching again) Send a telegram to beg for help, send a telegram to [counterattack], and establish a new position to lure the enemy deeper.······

Fifth stage: (The war situation in the front is unclear) [Avoid major sacrifices] and retreat to the Xth line of defense.

Sixth stage: Bundle up your children and wealth, retreat to Beiping, and send a telegram to the whole country, [preparing for long-term resistance].

If we [resist] according to such a [resistance plan], wouldn't our Chairman Tang immediately become a [national hero]? And weren't the garlands of many [national heroes] made in this way? But he didn't do that, and he had to simply abandon the city and flee. Being so stupid, is it not his fault that he was dismissed from office?

However, Tang Yulin has already [escaped], and he has [escaped to an unknown location]. Then, reading an Tang Yulin who is of unknown whereabouts to bear the total account of this [expected event] is ultimately beneficial to everyone, otherwise who should this account be charged to?

Swallows

— Mu Shiying

It was when twilight hung from the treetops, and there was a layer of purple haze in the sky, faint, like a seasonal dream. I walked slowly, until I reached a small river, and, leaning against the railing, I stood still. A gentle breeze blew past; I knew it was the wind of early spring. Such a tender wind of memory, and carried on the wind were one or two distant tolls from the Catholic church. Atop the church, the white cross silently clasped its hands in prayer beneath the vast purple sky, like a sacred virgin in a white robe.

A beam of sunset leaked through the leaves of the old willow tree in front of me, shining on my hairline; my hair had been tousled by the wind. And I softly whistled a tune, smiling. Such a tranquil, joyful twilight!

Suddenly I heard soft murmurs, whispering to each other. I raised my head and saw two purple swallows standing among the leaves of the old willow tree, fluttering their wings lightly, whispering their secrets of the South.

I looked at this pair of swallows; I recognized them. They and Miss Ling existed together in my memory. Miss Ling had already quietly lain beneath a piece of marble in the International Cemetery, which was inscribed with, [The Grave of Beloved Daughter Ouyang Ling]. But they had returned. Three years ago, I often saw this pair of purple swallows too. It was also spring then, also such a gentle wind, also such a tranquil twilight, also such a sacred white cross, also such a distant toll of the Catholic church. Miss Ling and I strolled slowly along this asphalt road in the suburbs. In the fields there was the scent of wheat, the double sound of cuckoos, the scorched fragrance of pine resin, a peaceful sky, peaceful sunlight—in the peaceful sky, under the peaceful sunlight, ripe fruits would fall peacefully. We would sit on the grass, on stone docks, on fallen flowers, on tree roots, we would stop by the bridge railing, and I would also gently whistle a tune, smiling. The pair of swallows would then stand in the willow branches above our heads, murmuring to each other, and Miss Ling would murmur to me just like the swallows. She could speak the language of swallows, whispering to each other, and she understood the secrets of the South, because she said:

"I am also a daughter of the South!"

She also said that the South had many, many purple swallows, which would often stand by her window and tell her about the scenery of her hometown. She said that several times, when she woke up in the morning and went to open the window, baby swallows would flutter in, flutter onto her, shivering. She also said that besides swallows, the South also had red beans, a blue sea, a clear sky, white buildings, and orchards.

She was suffering from homesickness! I knew she would eventually return one day.

That summer, she really did return, along with a pair of purple swallows. Now the purple swallows have returned twice, but where is Miss Ling? Where is Miss Ling? It is spring again, such a lovely twilight! The moon has risen, above the willow tips, on the beaks of the purple swallows.

I thought it would rain tomorrow. Sure enough, in the middle of that night, a few sparse drops of fine rain floated in from outside the window, floating into my sorrow, floating into my dreams.

May 3, Year 33

The Story of the Black Girl Seeking a Goddess (24)

— Written by George Bernard Shaw, Translated by Yi Xian

"There is no such goddess," said the image-maker. "There is no goddess but those that I make; and I have never made one called   ."

"She exists," said the black girl; "for the White Miss spoke of her reverently as the root of the female of the universe, which is incorporeal like number, and before the beginning, as God is before creation. It is not the sex of   ; it is from the female sex that the sex of    arises. The beginning must be something of this     from which we are made and to which we return when we return to earth. I used to puzzle when I was a little child over every number to find out how number one comes; because all the other numbers are only so many ones and so many ones; but what is one? I could not think. Now I know from    that one is increased by itself, not by marriage of male and female. When you have one you know why there is no beginning and end; because if you subtract one and one and one forever you never get to the beginning; and if you add one and one and one forever you never get to the end; and so you have found the eternal in number."

"The eternal alone is nothing," said the Arab. "What is the eternal to me if I cannot find the eternal truth?"

"The truth of number alone is eternal," said the black girl. "All other truths either pass away or become errors like the fancies of our childhood; but one and one are two, and one and ten are eleven, forever. Therefore there is something godlike in number."

"You cannot eat number, you cannot drink number," said the image-maker. "You cannot marry number."

"God will provide us with other things to eat and drink," said the black girl. "We can marry one another."

"Oh, you cannot even make a picture of it, let alone speak of it," said the image-maker.

"We Arabs can," said the Arab. "By this sign we shall conquer the world. See!" He stooped and wrote numbers in the sand.

"The priests say that God is the magic number of three in one and one in three," said the black girl.

"It is simple," said the Arab. "I am the son of my father and the father of my sons and with myself the three are one and the one is three. The nature of man is manifold: only God is One. He is Unity. He is, as you say, a thing increased by itself from itself. He is the heart of the void, the center of nothingness without which there can be no body. He is the number of the innumerable stars: the measure of the unmeasurable air!"

The Gold Rush Continues

The morning market was full of astonishing changes

The afternoon market settled into a dull state

8.2 taels strong, fluctuating up 6.7 taels

Although the gold market fell slightly in the morning, its rebound was extremely strong. Foreign telegrams showed that both near-term and long-term contracts rose. The near-term rose 4.375, and the long-term rose by half a penny. New York silver prices rose by 0.625, so the opening raw price was initially bid at 75 to 80 taels. The foreign exchange market also hardened accordingly. The initial bid price for near-term British exchange was 1 shilling 9.25 pence, and the US exchange was 33.125 yuan, easing to .375 and .1875. The opening price was 680 taels, then fell to 77.2 taels, and then rebounded strongly, mainly because the foreign exchange market tightened, with June US dollars difficult to settle at 34.5 yuan (75 in raw trading). Gold prices were pulled up to over 80 taels. Although there was a lot of maneuvering after this, the trend was very firm. The Dalian gang frantically bought Dalian contracts, and Japanese brokers stuffed Dalian contracts to advance shillings. Western merchants sold shillings to buy US dollars. Step by step, the foreign exchange market improved. In addition, retail investors covered their short positions and went long, so gold prices remained high. The market seemed dry, with major players advancing incessantly. June US dollars even traded at 33.625 yuan, with banks all accepting. HSBC's listed shilling exchange rate was reduced by .25, then jumped to outside the 700 taels mark, reaching 705.5 taels in a rush. Unfortunately, this good situation did not last long. Foreign telegrams reported that the US banking industry would extend its holiday again. Amidst this extended holiday announcement, cash exports were still prohibited. At this point, the gold market turned around, with many people selling off at high prices. A selling atmosphere permeated for a time, and prices plummeted by about 10 taels, retreating to 696.5 taels at the close. The afternoon was extremely flat, with sparse trading and a dull market. After the opening, prices rose due to a report of a 14-anna drop in Bombay, but still gradually, reaching 9.7 taels before stopping. There were still quite a few sellers. Although the foreign exchange market was flat, it was firm, gradually falling to 4.2 taels. Banks' appetite turned to acceptance, with shillings being particularly good, once reaching 701 taels. In the end, it was still flat. Bombay rebounded by 5 annas, then fell to 696.7 taels at the close. The trend seemed stable after the mid-day drop and rebound. There was a lot of hedging activity, selling US exchange to hedge term transfers. There were no transactions in spot transfers, with prices approximately the same. Abolished Cent, Japanese Silver Dollar Swap Interest Also Opens

丨Both the morning and afternoon markets are at 4 fen丨

Yesterday, the Ministry ordered the abolition of the market price of foreign cents. The conversion rate of silver dollars to foreign dollars is 7 qian 1 fen 5 li. From now on, there is no need to do market prices between markets, nor is there any need for ups and downs. At the same time, a kind of foreign dollar swap was added, but it was opened in conjunction with silver swaps. Yesterday, both the morning and afternoon markets were at 4 fen. If the foreign dollar swap is 4 fen, the silver swap is also 4 fen. All transfers are no longer fixed. The amount of foreign exchange drafts made was 1.35 million in the morning market and 910,000 in the afternoon market. Most foreign silver was in short supply and was generally distributed and evened out by the Money Industry Public Treasury. There were no reports of banknotes in either market. The total amount of check transactions in both markets was 145,000. There were no reports of bank transactions. Banknote inflows and outflows exceeded 900,000. All foreign accounts' dealings and foreign dollar swaps were simultaneously cancelled, and foreign dollar swaps were only swapped, not lent. Yesterday, foreign dollar swap drafts were about 2 million, and silver dollar swap drafts were over 2 million. Money shops' foreign public bills were increasingly cleared from then on, exceeding 18 million yesterday, while silver public bills were cleared less, only exceeding 14 million. Foreign exchange head bills were cleared for over 3.5 million, and silver exchange head bills were cleared for over 2.5 million. Bank clearing was also done in both silver and foreign dollars. Yesterday, silver dollar clearing, including commercial clearing bills, was over 2.1 million, and foreign clearing bills exceeded 2.34 million. Various commodity exchange taxes totaled over 7 million, with 500,000 in warehouse entries and 300,000 in warehouse exits. Foreign dollar clearing, the Chinese and foreign sides were too tied up with procedures, so there was not enough time to investigate the exact amount. The amount of small money shops' transactions was over 1.8 million, and the amount of foreign collateral loans was over 1.5 million. The amount of silver collateral loans was not detailed. The currency market situation was as follows: Jiangnan small foreign dollars were priced at 6 qian 1 fen 7 li and a half in the morning market and the same price in the afternoon market. Transactions were 5,000 jiao in the morning market and 4,000 jiao in the afternoon market. Guangdong small foreign dollars were priced at 5 qian 8 fen 1 li 8 hao 7 hu and a half in the morning market and 5 qian 8 fen 2 li in the afternoon market. Food

Wheat Futures Moved by the Label Flour

Yesterday, after the opening of wheat futures in the morning, the market for each month was extremely quiet, with only slight trading in March and July, and the rest were empty calls. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, because foreign wheat quotations were small, and the flour market in the morning also saw a large amount of activity, people's sentiment was not good, and selling was smooth. This situation was purely driven by the flour market, because the buyers are all laymen, and have no real ability to take delivery of goods. As a result, this month fell by three points, April fell by one point, July fell by three points, and August fell by two points.

Canadian Wheat Reported Down, Label Flour Fell Sharply

丨Tianjin Businesses and Factories Have Filed丨

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, each month presented a tragic decline. Canadian wheat quotations were also down about 0.03 yuan, and since the sharp drop in gold prices, there seemed to be another opportunity for selling foreign wheat. Australian wheat asking prices were as low as 3.38 yuan, and although the situation in the north had turned from danger to safety, the overall situation was still not optimistic. Therefore, all markets in Tianjin had filed. Large and small factories also continued to sell smoothly due to the loosening of foreign wheat and the remaining chips. Therefore, people's hearts were greatly discouraged, and everyone sold off. General speculative short positions also filed as much as possible, resulting in a considerable decline in each month. In the future, if foreign wheat floods the market or there are signs of further loosening, March and April will fall by 1.5 fen compared to the previous day, May will fall by 2.25 fen, June and July will fall by 2.5 fen, and August will fall by 2 fen.

Silk and Tea

Wuyuan Tea Industry Declines

In recent years, the Wuyuan tea industry has suffered losses due to the decline in sales of Russian Zhuang Gongxi and the impact of various Lu Ke competing to make extracted core tea, resulting in large losses for merchants. Recently, due to the tightening of loans by tea houses, weak capital, and the difficulty of maintaining tea companies, it is expected that this year's number of tea houses on this route will be reduced by 50-60 compared with last year, and most will reduce their business scope. The decline of the tea industry can be seen. However, it is heard that some Wuyuan gang tea merchants believe that if the Wuyuan tea industry wants to survive, it must advance the picking period. A vigorous campaign is currently underway to achieve this goal.

The US President Persists in Eliminating the Financial Crisis

Investigating Sound Banks Nationwide to Allow Resumption of Business

Requesting Congress to Reduce Pensions and Political Expenses

The Gold Ban Will Continue to Be Strictly Enforced

Reuters Washington, 10th: President Roosevelt today signed an order instructing Treasury Secretary Woodin to grant licenses to member banks of the Federal Reserve System that are sound, allowing them to resume operations. However, the gold ban will still be strictly enforced. Non-member state banks must obtain the approval of the state bank authorities before they can reopen. Treasury Secretary Woodin declared that twelve central Federal Reserve banks will reopen for business on the . Secretary of State Hull stated that once the domestic banking difficulties are resolved, the US government will begin diplomatic talks with various countries to lay the foundation for a successful world economic and financial conference.

Reuters Washington, 10th: After his victory yesterday, President Roosevelt is now persisting in attacking the payment of pensions to veterans in his economic plan. The bill was submitted to the Senate today, requesting Congress to immediately reduce this expenditure for those who have not completely lost their ability to serve and are still able to audit accounts. Although the President did not explain the detailed methods, it is estimated semi-officially that 300,000,000 yuan can be saved annually. President Roosevelt also asked Congress to allow him to reduce the salaries of government civil servants, up to a maximum of 15 percent, which is expected to save 450 million yuan annually. The shortfall in national expenditure for the 1933 fiscal year will exceed 1,200,000,000 yuan (excluding loans from the Financial Reconstruction Corporation). If no action is taken immediately for the 1934 national expenditure, the shortfall will be around 1,000,000,000 yuan, and short-term government bonds worth hundreds of millions of yuan must be repaid in the spring, so reform is urgent.

Havas Washington, 10th: Treasury Secretary Woodin declared that twelve Federal Reserve Banks will resume business tomorrow. The Presidential decree on the reopening of banks and the indefinite extension of the gold export ban was unanimously approved by Congress today. American banks can now be divided into three levels: the first level, 5,000 banks, is fully solvent; the second level, 4,000 banks, is in a stable position, but the Treasury Department will investigate their creditworthiness; the third level is all other small banks, and it is generally expected that these small banks will not be able to recover after closing.

Havas Washington, 10th: President Roosevelt's request to Congress to reduce the maintenance fees for World War veterans has prompted veterans to send telegrams to members of Congress to protest. As a result, some members of both the Senate and the House of Representatives have launched a movement against the President's request, but Democratic leaders are confident that Roosevelt will achieve a final victory.

US Senators Resume Silver Coinage Movement

Advocating Government Purchase of Silver to Raise Silver Prices

Reuters Washington, 10th: Senator Pittman has now resumed his silver coinage movement in the Senate. Pitt has reintroduced two bills that he proposed in the previous Congress: one is to allow the United Kingdom to use silver to pay off its war debts to the United States, limited to 100 million yuan, with a maximum of four shillings and five pence per ounce; the other is to allow the government to purchase domestic silver, 5 million ounces per month, and issue this coupon at the same time, so that it can become another standard for US currency. The second proposal by Senator Pittman has already been approved by the Senate Banking Committee. Now Pitt has also proposed a third proposal, advocating that the government purchase silver worth 250,000,000 yuan on the open market. Pitt believes that this move can eliminate the existing silver surplus and allow the price of silver to rise with the application of economic laws. Purchases will stop when the price of silver rises to 1.29 yuan per ounce.

Others mentioned Article 43 of the Treaty of Versailles, which stated that all German military exercises, as well as the stationing or assembly of troops, whether temporary or permanent, are prohibited in the entire left bank of the Rhine River and the area on the right bank within fifty kilometers from the river bank.

Song Ziwen's Talk This Morning

National Mobilization to Resist to the End

Chairman Chiang Decides to Sit in North China and Preside

Yan Feng and the Southwest are United in Resisting Japan, Regardless of Boundaries

Compromise and Direct Negotiations are All Japanese Propaganda

War Between the Two Countries Cannot Be Proportioned by Armaments

Song Ziwen, the Acting President of the Executive Yuan, flew north earlier to participate in the Baoding Conference. After deciding on the major military and financial plans for North China, he returned to Shanghai by the original plane at 2 pm yesterday. This newspaper reporter specially visited his residence on Qiqi Road at 11 am this morning. Song said that the military plan for North China has been decided, and no matter what, we will resist to the end. Even if the Japanese army can capture Nanjing, our determination to resist will not change in the slightest. He also refuted rumors of compromise, direct negotiations, and neutral zones, saying that under these circumstances, there is absolutely no possibility of negotiation. His attitude was extremely激昂. The following is a record of his conversation:

Fierce Fighting Outside the Pass

The reporter first asked what the recent situation in North China was like. Song replied, "The fighting outside Gubeikou is extremely fierce. Sun Dianying's troops are also fighting with the enemy in the . Sun's troops are poorly equipped, but they are able to engage in hand-to-hand combat with the enemy, causing heavy casualties to the enemy. The soldiers are loyal and brave, and they deserve to be commended. The rear of Sun's troops can be supplied from Dolun and has not been cut off by the Japanese army, so they will not be surrounded by the enemy."

Military Plan Decided

When asked about the results of the Baoding Conference, he replied, "Chiang Kai-shek, Zhang Xueliang and I met in Baoding to discuss the military and financial plans for North China, which have been largely decided. As for the approval of Zhang Xueliang's resignation, there is currently no clear order from the Central Government." He was also asked whether the arrangements for the Northeast Army to be transferred to the rear and the Central Army to be transferred to the front were also decided at the meeting. He replied, "Now that we are resisting Japan, all the soldiers in the country are united, and there is no distinction between the Northeast Army and the Central Army."

Yan Feng is United in Resisting Japan

When asked about Yan Feng's attitude and whether they planned to meet with Chiang Kai-shek, Song replied, "Yan's representative, Xu Yongchang, met with Chiang Kai-shek in Shijiazhuang this time, and the result was very satisfactory. Mr. Feng supports extreme resistance, so he fully agrees with the military plan." He was also asked whether Yan Feng organized civilian groups in Zhangjiakou and planned to go to the front line to kill the enemy. Song said that he had not heard of it. He asked whether Feng would take up anti-Japanese military work and under what name. He replied that he was not sure.

National Soldiers Kill the Enemy

When asked whether the Southwest's dispatch of troops to resist Japan could be realized, he replied, "Now the whole country is completely united against foreign aggression. The troops of all provinces are willing to go to the front line to kill the enemy, and there is no distinction between the Southwest and the Central Government. While the soldiers are killing the enemy on the front line, I hope that the people in the rear will also actively carry out anti-Japanese work, uniting from top to bottom to jointly cope with this unprecedented national crisis."

British Mediation is Not True

When asked whether it was heard that Reuters reported that the British Ambassador Lampson was going to mediate again and that the Japanese had proposed to designate the area along the Great Wall from Yuguan to Gubeikou as a neutral zone, he replied, "Absolutely not. Under the current circumstances, compromise and direct negotiations are all propaganda released by the Japanese to ease international scrutiny. No matter what, we will resist to the end. Wherever the Japanese army goes, resistance will follow. Even if the Japanese army can capture Nanjing, our determination to resist and our military plan will not change."

Fight to the Death with the Enemy

When asked, "In your previous speech, you said that our army is from the 17th and 18th centuries and cannot fight the Japanese army. I am afraid that this resistance will repeat the mistakes of Rehe. What do you think?" Song resolutely replied, "This is precisely my strongest expression. Resistance cannot be judged by success or failure. Victory is gratifying, and we will continue to fight even if we fail. Moreover, what I call the army of the 17th and 18th centuries refers to the troops of Tang Yulin. There are many excellent troops in the country, and we cannot generalize. We should take the Rehe incident as a lesson and improve the weaknesses of our army so that we can kill the enemy and win. Moreover, war between the two countries cannot be precisely observed based on the superiority or inferiority of armaments or the strength of the army. For example, if Germany has a six-inch caliber cannon that is more numerous than the French, will France surrender because of this? Or if the number of British battleships is several times that of Japan, will Japan immediately surrender? Therefore, if we compare the strength of armaments and troops, there is no war to be fought between the two countries. Our country's situation is exactly like this. We should use the courage of the nation, the unity of the people, and fight to the death with the enemy, using the flesh and blood of the nation to open a way out. Therefore, today is the only opportunity for our country's revival. Life and death, survival and extinction, depend on this one move."

Song Will Not Go North Temporarily

Song also said, "Since President Wang went abroad, I have been acting as the President of the Executive Yuan. Now President Wang will return to China on the 17th and arrive in Shanghai. After that, there will be someone responsible for all major political plans. I will devote myself to planning finances. Therefore, I will not go north temporarily. Chiang Kai-shek, the chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, plans to reside in North China to command the military. Although the military expenditure in North China is not very abundant, it is already sufficient to cope with it."

Punish Negligent Generals

As for the punishment of the responsible generals for the fall of Rehe, Tang Yulin has been arrested by the government. As for other generals such as Zhang Zuoxiang, I have not discussed it in detail with Chiang Kai-shek and Zhang Xueliang because I stayed in the north for a very short time. I do not know how to deal with it. In short, the Central Government will have the fairest way to clarify rewards and punishments, maintain discipline, and boost morale.

Plan to Recover Lost Territory

The reporter also asked whether the Central Government's so-called military plan was only to resist and stop there, and how to recover the lost territory and whether to counterattack Chengde. He replied, "Chiang Kai-shek's determination to resist has been detailed in his talks with reporters in Zhengzhou. As for the recovery of lost territory and the counterattack against Chengde, it depends on the progress of the military. I am not a military expert, so I do not know the detailed plan."

Zhang Xueliang Comes to Shanghai

Today, there is a rumor that Zhang Xueliang is coming to Shanghai by plane. The reporter took the opportunity to ask about it. Song said, "There is no telegram to Shanghai this morning." He was also asked about the situation in Beiping and Tianjin, which is very tense. Will the Japanese army really seize North China? He replied, "We do not ask how the Japanese army is progressing. Wherever the Japanese army goes, resistance will follow. The Central Government has already made up its mind."

Zeng Zhongming Goes to Hong Kong This Morning to Welcome Wang

The Railway Department's Issuance of Public Bonds is Postponed Due to the Suspension of Boxer Indemnity Payments

Cleaning Up the Outstanding Foreign Debt of 1.3 Billion Yuan Will Proceed

President of the Executive Yuan Wang Jingwei and his wife are returning to China on the French mail ship Aramis, which will pass through Hong Kong on the 14th and arrive in Shanghai on the 17th. Ministers from all departments of the Executive Yuan will come to Shanghai to welcome Wang. Zeng Zhongming, the Vice Minister of Railways, took the French ship Baodaosi to Hong Kong at around 10 am this morning to welcome Wang. According to Zeng's statement to the New Voice Agency reporter, the Railway Department borrowed money from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Committee to complete the Yuehan Railway and issued 1,220,000 pounds of public bonds. Recently, it has been suspended due to the suspension of Boxer Indemnity payments for one year. It will find other ways to complete it. The total amount of foreign debt owed by Chinese railways to various countries in the past is extremely huge. According to the report of the Ministry of Finance, the principal and interest have now reached more than 1.3 billion yuan, of which British and Belgian loans account for the majority. The Railway Department has decided to clean it up because it has such a huge amount of foreign debt, and even just the interest that should be paid each year requires about 100 million yuan, so it has decided to clean it up so that it can find ways to gradually repay it in the future. The relocation of the North Station and the land acquisition have also been suspended for the time being, and will be determined after seeking the opinions of the ministers of the Executive Yuan. According to Wang's previous telegram, he is not yet fully recovered. It is not yet certain whether he will return to Beijing to take office immediately after arriving in Shanghai. Song Ziwen, the Acting President of the Executive Yuan, originally intended to go to Europe to attend the World Economic Conference, but it is unlikely to be realized due to the current national crisis, and it has been largely suspended. It is said that Zeng will arrive in Hong Kong tomorrow morning and come to Shanghai on the same ship after meeting Wang the next day. Zeng had notified Wang by radio before leaving.

The Future of the Disarmament Conference is Bleak

France and Germany Hold Diametrically Opposed Views

Britain Finds Mediation Extremely Difficult

Geneva, 10th (Reuters) – The darkness of the Disarmament Conference's future and the hopelessness of reaching an agreement have never been as pronounced as they are today. British Prime Minister MacDonald is about to arrive in Geneva at this very moment. On any important matter concerning disarmament, a complete deadlock is evident between France and Germany, with neither side showing any sign of compromise. Germany believes that since it has disarmed, it bears no responsibility. What it demands, whether it be armament or disarmament, is simply equality. France, on the other hand, states that the extent of France's disarmament must be governed by the degree of security that France obtains. The conflict in viewpoints is evident on every issue in the conference, regardless of whether the discussion concerns troop numbers, weapons, air forces, or the abolition of war. Making the Prime Minister's task even more difficult is the absence of key officials from Germany, France, and Italy. Germany is unwilling to send Chancellor von Papen or Foreign Minister Neurath until it receives concrete proposals. French Premier Daladier is also unwilling to risk being besieged by a united front of Britain, the United States, and Italy in Geneva. Italy has expressed great sympathy and attention but has not explicitly declared its support for Germany's position. However, the recent resolution of the Fascist Grand Council has confirmed Italy's stance. At the same time, the rapprochement between Poland and Soviet Russia is now apparent, and this has led to a closer understanding between France and Russia. This shift has been prompted by German Chancellor Hitler's anti-communist actions. Considering all the aforementioned circumstances, Prime Minister MacDonald hopes to obtain some form of agreement or, at least, a supplementary agreement for an armaments truce. However, even this approach will be strongly opposed by Germany, making the future extremely bleak.

British Authorities Depart Paris for Geneva

Official Statement Acknowledges Tensions in the Disarmament Issue

Determined to Seek International Compromise to Maintain Peace

Paris, 10th – Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Secretary Simon have departed for Geneva. French Premier Daladier intends to visit Geneva early next week at their specific request. Today, after MacDonald, Daladier, Poncet, and Simon concluded their discussions, they stated that they were quite optimistic. After the meeting, a public statement was issued, stating that all members fully acknowledged the urgency of the Geneva issue, especially in relation to the current situation in Europe. All members declared their determination to seek a compromise with other countries to preserve world peace.

German Representative's Security Demands

Hopes for a Practical Resolution at the Conference

Geneva, 10th (Havas) – The German representative to the Disarmament Conference, Nadolny, published an article in "The League of Nations Journal," concluding that "Germany has already disarmed and is extremely vulnerable to insecurity. Therefore, Germany must formally reject any proposals to postpone the Disarmament Conference and seek other temporary solutions. For thirteen years, Germany has been waiting for all countries to implement disarmament as stipulated in the Treaty of Versailles in order to restore security. The Disarmament Conference has been working for fourteen months, and the time has come to take real decisions. We are compelled to demand a practical resolution from the Disarmament Conference."

Italian Premier Encourages Blackshirt Comrades

Rome, 10th (Havas) – The Fascist Party leadership held a meeting last night, chaired by Prime Minister Mussolini. The Prime Minister declared that Italy's political goal is not to disturb world peace but to assist in the political, economic, and spiritual reconstruction of Europe. He also stated that if the Disarmament Conference abandons Italy's specific proposals, it will not achieve positive results. The Prime Minister urged all Italian Blackshirts to strive for the strength of the nation and to spread Fascism throughout the world.

Political Committee Discusses Definition of Aggressor

Majority Supports Soviet Russian Proposal

British and American Representatives Express Doubts

Japanese and German Representatives are Guilt-Ridden

Geneva, 10th (Reuters) – The Political Committee of the Disarmament Conference met this afternoon to discuss the Soviet Russian proposal regarding the definition of an aggressor. Russian representative Dovgalevsky stated that only complete disarmament could guarantee security, but since the Soviet Union's proposal to achieve this goal has not gained support, he believed it was necessary to define a strict method to naturally determine who is the aggressor. Chinese representative Dr. Lo Chung-yi stated that he believed the issue of applying Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant should also be studied, and the current situation in the Far East proves the importance of this issue. He expressed his agreement with the Russian plan and deeply regretted the lack of a solution to the problem of undeclared wars. If such a solution existed, China would not be suffering as it is today. Several speakers supported the Russian proposal, but France gave it limited approval. British representative Eden and American representative Whitehouse expressed doubts about whether such a strict definition of an aggressor could be implemented or whether it would be beneficial. Japanese representative Yada stated that the definition of an aggressor would often involve various difficult problems that must be considered and disputed, requiring difficult investigations. He argued that a fair method focusing on practicality should be sought. After repeated discussions, the Political Committee assigned a drafting committee to draft clauses for further discussion.

Geneva, 10th (Havas) – The Soviet Russian representative has submitted a proposal to the Disarmament Conference regarding the definition of an aggressor. This afternoon, the Political Committee of the Disarmament Conference will present the proposal for discussion. The Soviet Russian representative believes that the definition of an aggressor should be issued in the form of a declaration, which should be global in nature and included in the Security and Disarmament Convention, or as a separate compromise and considered part of the Disarmament Convention. This declaration would regard all hostile actions, except formal declarations of war, that have not undergone the declaration of war procedure as acts of aggression. The Soviet Russian representative stated that the more automatically it can be proven who is the aggressor in international conflicts, the more international peace will benefit. This aligns with France's opinion. This proposition of the Soviet Russian representative was generally welcomed, with China, Norway, Poland, Ireland, and France supporting it, while the United States criticized it.

"National Soul Eliminates Traitors" Group Member Liu Chongwu and Others Appeal

Trial Opens This Morning

Adjourned for Further Hearing

Liu Chongwu and other members of the "National Soul Eliminates Traitors" group, angered by traitorous merchants privately selling enemy goods and undermining the patriotic movement, gathered comrades and went to various traitorous merchants to warn them. When the merchants refused to listen, the group gave them bombs or opened fire, resulting in injuries and deaths. The police arrested Liu and several others, and the Special District Court filed charges against them for conspiracy to murder. After investigation, Liu Chongwu was sentenced to seven years of imprisonment. Pan Hongsheng, Cao Songsheng, Tian Shuiyang, Zhu Erkang, and Hua Zhongyuan, whose involvement was minor, were sentenced to imprisonment ranging from four months to one month. Tian and Zhu were both granted a two-year suspended sentence. Details have been reported previously. It is now learned that Liu Chongwu, dissatisfied with the verdict, has filed an appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court through his defense lawyers Fan Gang and Chen Tingrui. The Municipal Council also considered the sentences imposed on the defendants to be too lenient and has filed an appeal with the High Court. This morning, Judge Zhou Han of the Criminal Division of the Second Branch of the High Court specially opened the Second Tribunal, summoned witnesses, and conducted a hearing on Liu's case. Judge Zhou assigned lawyer Fan Gang and others to defend the other appellants, as they were unable to hire lawyers themselves, to protect their legal interests. The Municipal Council's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, first stated the reasons for appealing against the first-instance judgment. The court then questioned each of the defendants in turn. Liu and others generally stated that they were warning the traitorous merchants because they were angry about their private sale of enemy goods. They either completely denied or claimed self-defense in relation to the shooting of Wang Zhengqing, manager of Maotai Foreign Goods Store on Xinzha Road, Wang Yirong, partner of Yuyuanheng Foreign Goods Store on Hankou Road, and the bombing and injury of Ku Bin Tai. The court then summoned witnesses for testimony. The court adjourned until noon, and Liu and others were returned to custody for further hearing at a later date.

The "Lichuan" Steamer on the Suzhou-Hangzhou Route Robbed for the Second Time

Robbed Near Lake Tai

Please Urge the Water Police Bureau to Arrest the Bandits

The "Lichuan" steamer of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company on the Suzhou-Hangzhou route was robbed last month, as reported in this newspaper. Recently, the ship was robbed by bandits for the second time. The captain of the steamer has reported the incident to Shanghai. According to the report, the "Lichuan" steamer departed from Hangzhou on the 3rd of this month with only twenty passengers, mostly women. Around 2 a.m. on the morning of the 4th, when the ship was near Linghu, it was dark. As the "Lichuan" passed, bandits who had been lying in wait along the riverbanks fired warning shots and ordered the ship to stop. The captain had no choice but to stop the engine. Six or seven bandits boarded the ship, first guarding the people on board and then proceeding to rob them. None of the passengers were spared. The captain, the purser, and others were also searched. Even small silver coins, copper coins, jewelry, and clothing were taken. Because there were not many passengers, and they were all poor, less than two hundred yuan was stolen. No one was injured. Before leaving, the bandits shouted that their luck was bad. Later, when the "Lichuan" arrived in Suzhou and docked, the passengers were in a state of disarray. The captain has reported the incident to the Shanghai office, which has reported it to the Inland Water Police Bureau, urging them to arrest the bandits and to send police to protect the Suzhou-Hangzhou route.

Science

Nicotine

— Quiet

It is almost universally known that cigarettes are harmful, because the toxins they contain are sufficient to ruin a person's potential, drain a person's vitality, dull a person's senses, and deaden a person's thoughts. All of a person's ambitions, intelligence, and profound understanding can be dissolved and exhausted by smoking cigarettes. The intensity of the harm is truly startling!

It has been found that cigarettes contain eighteen kinds of toxins, and the most poisonous of them is nicotine. This substance is not found in ordinary food, nor is it included in protoplasm. Now, a brief description of it is given below: (1) Where Nicotine is Located

Nicotine, also known as 菸　, belongs to the alkaloids in organic chemistry. It often combines with malic acid and citric acid to form organic salts, which are stored in tobacco, tea, and their seeds. Its content is about 0.28　. Good quality ordinary cigarettes contain about 2　, while inferior ones contain more　.

(2) Extraction of Nicotine

The nicotine in tobacco leaves can be extracted by the following method: soak the tobacco leaves in hot water, boil them, mix them with milk of lime, and put them in a distillation flask with a condenser and a receiver. Then, add oxalic acid to the distillate to make it acidic, then evaporate it to concentrate it, and decompose it with potassium hydroxide to obtain free nicotine, which can be extracted with ether.

In ordinary laboratories, the following method is used for testing:

Take one cigarette, 25 CC of water, and 2 CC of dilute sulfuric acid, place them in a small distillation flask, heat to boiling, and after ten minutes, add an excess of sodium hydroxide deep solution, distill it, and then take the distillate and add various tests.

(3) Properties of Nicotine

Nicotine is a reddish oily liquid that boils at 247o C, with a strong irritating taste and an unpleasant odor. When exposed to air, it turns yellow and brown, eventually becoming a resinous liquid. It is extremely toxic, and only two or three drops can take a person's life within a few minutes. It is easily soluble in water, alcohol, solution, trapped liquid, and petroleum ether. When ignited, it mostly decomposes into carbonic acid, water, and nitrogen.

(4) Harms of Nicotine

It is common knowledge that cigarettes are poisonous, yet people still compete to smoke them, as if cigarettes can replace food. This is tantamount to self-harming one's body and mind, dulling one's intelligence, and blocking one's cleverness. Once nicotine is inhaled, it immediately flows into the blood and spreads throughout the nervous system. If someone without a nicotine addiction smokes it, they will experience dizziness, which is clear evidence that the nerves are being anesthetized. Those who smoke excessively will have trembling fingers, which shows that nicotine damages the nerves significantly. There is also the so-called "tobacco heart," which causes rapid pulse and palpitations. The reason is entirely due to the toxicity of nicotine, which directly affects the nerve cells in the cardiac nerve ganglion. Even worse is "tobacco blindness," which causes a person's eyesight to lose the sense of light in certain areas, gradually leading to blindness. Its danger is self-evident. In addition, nicotine is also harmful to the vocal cords. When smoking, the gas or dust from the smoke must pass through the opening between the two vocal cords in the larynx. The sensation of the outer layer of the vocal cords is very sensitive. Prolonged stimulation by smoke will gradually thicken it, resulting in a hoarse voice and an inability to speak or sing loudly! This harm is especially severe for opium smokers. In addition to this, smokers experience several other negative phenomena, such as a yellow and bloodless complexion, declining memory, reduced appetite, insomnia at night, fingers stained with nicotine, a mouth full of smoke odor, and the waste of useful money in useless places, which is truly regrettable!

The harmfulness of cigarettes has been described above. I sincerely hope that the people of our country will pay attention to it.

Literature and Art

Eulogy for Martyr Xu Zhongshu

— Sun Choucheng

Comrade Xu Zhongshu of the Soviet Army died in battle in Guangdong. In addition to building a memorial tower in Jinshan Park, it is planned to bury his clothes and hat to comfort his spirit in the afterlife. This is written to express grief.

The Qing government was corrupt and about to collapse. Witnessing this with heartache, he seized the opportunity to rise up. With ardent passion and a determination to restore order, he worked with the Soviet Army, discussing military strategies. He was humble in learning, deeply admired for his diligence, and well-versed in the Six Secret Teachings, with outstanding intelligence. During the Xinhai Revolution, he returned to his hometown, and I followed Director Cheng to serve on the battlefield, guarding the neighborhoods and suppressing the Zhang bandits. Although our work was different, we were united in our struggle. After the failure of the Guichou Revolution, he went into hiding in his hometown. Although he took up teaching, he never forgot his mission to eliminate traitors. When Yuan Shikai was punished by heaven, he resumed his writing and, angered by the chaotic state of the government, fled south. He rejoined the army during the Southwestern Protection Movement, holding important positions in eastern Guangdong. Before the Gui rebels were eliminated, hindering the Northern Expedition, he first went on a western expedition, hoping to eliminate the warlords. The rebel army was stubborn, spying on Yangjiang. In imminent danger, filled with loyalty and indignation, the isolated army had no support. The sound of sighs frequently echoed within. Seeing this situation, he was the first to respond to the call, and his momentum grew, quickly forming a battalion. He registered names late into the night and was elected captain, making plans that very evening. Heavy rain poured down as the rebel enemies ran rampant. Raising his arms, he charged to kill the enemy, dying in battle from a bullet. Coffin made of wooden boards, a knife used to inscribe a stone, buried bones on Nine Ridge, no horse hide to wrap the body. Time flies, and eight years have suddenly passed. Remembering the martyrs, hoping to comfort their spirits in the afterlife, we bury his clothes and hat, with a tomb five feet high. Alas, Xu Jun, your loyal soul and righteous spirit.

Bernard Shaw's Overthinking

— Tianfang

The day before yesterday, newspapers reported that Irish humorist Bernard Shaw entertained reporters in Beiping. In addition to stating in an article that he had "no mission" in coming to the East, he also expressed his opinions on the Manchurian issue. According to a Reuters reporter, "[The millions of Chinese in Manchuria must become Irish-style Nationalists, that is, each Chinese must be guarded by one Japanese soldier with a rifle. This is, of course, impossible."

This so-called humorous Irishman is extremely insightful on this matter. His words are subtle and can make people smile bitterly. But when he crossed the ocean, he seemed to have forgotten to bring a pair of glasses, so his observations of China are somewhat inaccurate. Leaving aside his other arguments, what he said above is also overly optimistic.

Our China is large enough to be called a great power. Its 3.5 million square miles of land and 474 million people often shock foreigners. But being large and useless, like a pile of garbage, is nothing to boast about. The first main argument of general optimists ["China will not perish"] is "there are many people." Unexpectedly, the foreign Shaw was also poisoned by this. You should know that in the West, one hundred Irishmen are certainly not afraid of one hundred Asians, but in the East, 25,000 Englishmen can manage 350 million Indians. I remember that the demise of India, although directly caused by the East India Company, was indirectly completed by the Indians themselves. If there were not those Indian "traitors" who ate the "royal" salary and sucked the people's blood, I don't think the British could have destroyed India, nor could they have managed it even if they had destroyed it. What about our China? The population is said to be 400 million. If we were to have one guard for each person, then at least the entire Europe would have to be merged to deal with one China. But rest assured, the reality is definitely not as imagined. We have plenty of traitors waiting for the price, not necessarily good. Given the opportunity, they will take off their robes, put on prison uniforms, and become English sailors. Although their noses are not high enough, their skin is not white enough, and their gait is not majestic enough, they are more than enough to be ["XX Imperial Army"]. We already have some experience with this. Shaw's words are overthinking.

Here, we cannot but blame the hosts for their lack of consideration. When Shaw stepped on the Chinese coast, they did not give him a pair of "old-age" glasses.

Smiling, I Ask the Guest Where He Comes From

— Yuanxi

Young Madam Wu rarely went out, because all the family's social affairs were handled by Old Madam Wu.

One day, an unexpected guest suddenly entered. He held a bamboo cane, his clothes tattered, looking like a beggar. He sat down casually on the red sandalwood chair in the living room, coughed a few times loudly, and pulled out the dry tobacco pouch stuck in his collar to smoke.

"Hey! What are you doing, old man? Get out!" Young Madam Wu was so scared that she didn't know what to do.

"Um! I'm here to see A-Gui's mother." Then he coughed loudly a few more times.

"Why would he be looking for my mother-in-law!" Young Madam Wu was even more baffled. "Mom! Look at this annoying old man, a living Buddha who suddenly came in and sat down without moving!" She said to the old woman who happened to walk in.

"Who are you looking for?" The old woman sized him up and down.

"I'm looking for you!"

"What's your name?" The old woman was a little angry.

"Whatever your name is, that's my name," the old man said with a smile.

"Um..." The old woman stared at his face, even more confused, then suddenly seemed to discover something and exclaimed half a sentence: "This is A-Gui's..." but then stopped herself. Young Madam Wu could only stare blankly!

"Haha! You only recognize me now?" He put on an even more old-fashioned air.

"I don't believe it! You have to take off your jacket first and let me recognize the birthmark on your shoulder." After seeing it, he threw his heavy, heavily patched tattered jacket on the ground, saying with a mixture of anger and joy: "You old thing! You abandoned your wife and children and left home for more than thirty years, disappearing without a trace. I thought you were long gone! Now you're back, why are you still like this?"

"Sin, sin! Don't look down on it, my life's blood and sweat are in it!" So he quickly picked up the tattered jacket, holding it tightly as if it were a treasure: "Ever since I left my hometown that year and went to Fengtian, I originally wanted to be a farmer, but I was hired to go to the gold mines in Heilongjiang. Life in the cellar was really bitter! Fortunately, I could steal a little bit of gold every day to supplement my meager wages, but it wasn't easy to smuggle it out of the mining area."

"Why didn't you ever send any news?"

"Not to mention that I can't write letters, even if I could, it wouldn't be easy to send them. Year after year, until the Japanese devils came to seize the mines, I was finally able to disguise myself and escape. It's a pity that I still have most of the gold leaves hidden in the ground that I didn't have time to dig out, especially the inexhaustible mineral resources, which were all seized by the Japanese devils. Alas!"

"Gold leaves! Didn't you bring any back at all?"

"Although I didn't bring back much, it's enough for us to use for the rest of our lives!"

"Really? Show me the real thing!"

"This is it!" The old man smiled and handed the heavy tattered jacket back to the old woman, cutting open strands of worn-out batting, all filled with clusters of fragmented gold!

Alas, Civil Rights!

Clerk Communication

Renting Land Should Start with Self-Production

— Liu Jingzhu

It has been going on for a long time.

Editor,

I am currently a clerk in X Incense and Candle Shop. For the past ten years, my monthly salary has only been enough to make ends meet. The other day, a relative of mine came and said that he had found a better job and wanted to transfer the small shop he runs to me. The shop has a total capital of 2,000 yuan. He wants to withdraw half of it, and I would invest 1,000 yuan. All shop affairs and expenses would be my sole responsibility. I found that the shop is conveniently located and has been quite profitable in recent years, so I am very willing and consider it a rare opportunity. However, I still lack 200-300 yuan in cash, and I am thinking of selling an acre or so of ancestral land in my hometown to raise the money. But that land was rented to the Shen family by my great-grandfather. The Shen family has built two storefront houses on the land and, seven years ago, sublet it to the Yin family. The Yin family has also built several houses. Currently, the Shen family collects 36 yuan in rent from the Yin family annually, while I only get 4,000 cash annually, and there is no rental agreement. I have repeatedly asked for an increase in rent, but the Shen family has repeatedly delayed and avoided me, and has never been willing to meet and talk. Recently, they have become even more brazen and owe more than two years of rent. I can no longer tolerate it and have long wanted to find a solution. Now, because of the matter mentioned above, I have made up my mind to order the Shen and Yin families to sell the houses to me at a discount so that I can take back the land and sell it. Editor, I don't know if this method is appropriate? I would be grateful for your reply.

Sincerely, Liu Jingzhu

X X X X

Editor's Note: Since Mr. Liu recognizes that taking over this small shop is a rare opportunity, you certainly cannot let it pass. As for lacking 200-300 yuan in cash and planning to sell ancestral land in your hometown to raise the money, that is appropriate. However, according to your letter, although the money seems unlikely to fall through, it may not be easy to obtain in a short time. So, we believe that Mr. Liu, on the one hand, can certainly negotiate with the Shen and Yin families; on the other hand, it is best to find other ways to raise the money. Since your relative is willing to not completely withdraw his capital, he must have great faith in you. You can discuss it with him, and you can share the profits and losses equally. Can you ask him to lend you another 200-300 yuan? He should not completely refuse, right?

As for the rental negotiations with the Shen and Yin families, you do not have a rental agreement. We do not know if you have other documents to prove your ownership. Do you pay the land tax on this land? If there is no proof and you do not pay the tax, the future of the negotiations is hard to say. If you have sufficient documents, then your right to the land can be confirmed. However, you cannot order them to tear down the houses, because the law stipulates that unless there is a contract, the principle of "no demolition after completion" applies. In other words, you cannot ask them to tear down the houses they built. But you also cannot confiscate them, because you did not get this kind of contract! So even if you sue in court, you will inevitably have to buy them at a price. This matter may be different. Therefore, we believe that Mr. Liu should ask someone to tell the Shen family that you are willing to transfer the land to them. If they are really stubborn and unreasonable, then you can proceed with the lawsuit, and it is best to express your willingness to transfer the land in the complaint. As for the price, you can start by making an offer, and they can counteroffer. In the end, the judge can make a fair assessment.

Novel

Time in a Dream

— Qin Shouou

(1) A Shout After Waking Up

The day of XX month XX year of the Great Republic of China, the XX festival in Nanjing, our capital, was the most serious day. To put it more precisely, it could be said that this day was a matter of life and death that the Republic of China had never encountered in its history. The situation was equally serious throughout the country, and Nanjing was the seat of the central government, so the atmosphere was even more tense than elsewhere.

In the past, Nanjing was always as quiet and silent as a chaste widow who had vowed to remain faithful. The hustle and bustle of the Huaipailou Confucius Temple area was only her occasional, partial smile. On this day, although the singing in the Confucius Temple area had completely stopped due to the uneasy situation, and the shops in the Huaipailou area were all displaying signs of "expressing determination to fight, closing for one day," closing their doors like iron barrels, the whole of Nanjing was shrouded in a tense and enthusiastic atmosphere. The chaste widow had transformed into a female athlete on the sports field. On both sides of the street, three or four feet thick "walls of people" were piled up. From 1:00 PM to 6:00 or 7:00 PM, the "walls of people" never wavered. Everyone, men, women, old, and young, all exuded an extremely tragic and excited expression, waiting and discussing.

"Feng XX arrives in Nanjing! Cai XX sends troops..." Every one or two hours, newspaper vendors on bicycles and on foot would roll in like a whirlwind with a new batch of special editions, shouting the titles of important news items in voices that had already gone hoarse. Five thousand copies, ten thousand copies, twenty thousand copies, would be snatched up by the waiting people in less than twenty minutes!

Blood-red, fist-sized red characters were pasted high on the billboards at the intersections by the messengers and tea boys of the various newspapers, announcing the latest news. Before the person pasting them could even get down, the billboards were already surrounded.

The cars of news reporters flew madly on Zhongshan Road. The banners of "X Newspaper" and "X News Agency" in white cloth and black characters had the same effect as the sirens on fire trucks. Wherever the banners flew, all vehicles would humbly retreat to the side, allowing them to open their speed and take as much information as possible about the interim emergency meeting of the Central Executive Committee.

The interim emergency meeting of the Central Executive Committee was convened because X country sent an ultimatum. It was scheduled to be held in the afternoon of this day in the Mausoleum of Dr. Sun Yat-sen under Zijin Mountain. When the clock struck two, the important people in Nanjing and the important people outside Nanjing had all arrived gracefully, preparing to participate in this serious gathering to decide the strategy of war or peace.

"Hey! What are you doing?" Less than half an hour after the meeting began, a middle-aged man with extremely neat clothes suddenly came to the large stone square in front of Dr. Sun Yat-sen's mausoleum and calmly took out seven or eight very long and wide white cloths with large characters written on them, like funeral couplets, from a small rattan box he brought himself, and laid them one by one on the ground, alarming a guard.

"If you are a Chinese," the man handed a business card to the soldier, uttering a deeply pained voice, "if you don't want to be a slave of a conquered country, please don't interfere with me for the time being!"

The ten black characters "Wu Yi, President of National XX University" on the business card immediately stopped the guard's intervention. They all knew that Wu Yi was a famous educator, and at the very least, they knew that the president of a national university was an official and could not be easily offended. Therefore, they stood by with their hands tied, watching Wu Yi with a curious mind.

Wu Yi was a tall, handsome middle-aged man, and at this time, his face was as solemn as if covered with a layer of thick frost. After laying out the six or seven funeral couplet-like white cloths, he took out a bronze bell commonly used in schools from the small rattan box and shook it vigorously.

"Ding... Ling..."

"This won't do! This is not allowed!" The guards felt that this Dr. Wu was really making too much trouble and planned to step forward to implement military intervention.
